Important News

Chairman Chiang Kai-shek Sends Chiang Bo-cheng to Jinan 74

To Meet with Han Fu-qu on Important Matters Concerning North China, Jinan Correspondence: After President of the Executive Yuan Wang Jingwei resigned and went to Shanghai, the Pacification Commissioner of Peiping, Zhang Xueliang, also decisively retired based on Wang's telegram. Shandong Provincial Chairman Han Fu-qu is the center of gravity in North China. Therefore, Military Affairs Commission Chairman Chiang Kai-shek specially dispatched his representative stationed in Peiping, Chiang Bo-cheng, to Jinan to meet with Han for consultations. Chiang Bo-cheng boarded the 201 train on the Pingpu Line from Peiping on the 8th and arrived in Jinan at 9:00 am on the 9th. Han Fu-qu, heads of various provincial government departments, and members all went to the station to welcome him. After Chiang got off the train, he shook hands with each of the welcomers as a courtesy. He then rode in the same car with Han Fu-qu to the Central Bank and talked for over an hour before they parted. This reporter made a special visit to Chiang Bo-cheng and Han Fu-qu, and recorded their conversations as follows:

Chiang Bo-cheng said: President Wang suddenly resigned on the 6th. Director Zhang, who was responsible for military affairs in North China, also resigned in succession. Commander-in-Chief Chiang believes that at this critical time, when Rehe and Yuyu are under pressure, the successive retirements of Wang and Zhang may affect the overall situation in North China. Therefore, he sent me to Shandong to consult with Chairman Han, as he is the center of gravity in North China and is of great importance. I have just met with Mr. Han, and he has expressed that he will obey Commander-in-Chief Chiang as always. He will follow Commander-in-Chief Chiang's opinion at all times and in all matters. Regarding President Wang's resignation, he will send a telegram earnestly persuading him to return to the capital. As for Director Zhang's resignation, he deeply admires his open-minded attitude. As for Commander-in-Chief Chiang's opinion on this matter, I am far away in Peiping and have not heard anything yet. Last night, when I boarded the train in Peiping,

I called Director Zhang from the station, but he had not yet received a telegram from Commander-in-Chief Chiang. However, Director Zhang's resignation telegram had already been sent. According to the conversation when Zhang met with me, he was suffering and had no way out. President Wang ordered him to resign, which was exactly what he wanted. The report of demanding military funds is not true. Zhang may send a telegram to explain. The North China Political Affairs Commission will also send a telegram to testify. Important generals in North China, such as Xu Yongchang, Shang Zhen, Chuan Zuoyi, Pang Bingxun, Song Zheyuan, Sun Dianying, Yu Xuezhong, Zhang Zuoxiang, and Wang Shuchang, are all in Peiping and have not expressed their opinions on Zhang's resignation. As for Wang's resignation, they agree with Zhang and will send a telegram to retain him. Before the Central Government approves Zhang's resignation, military affairs will be handled by the Military Affairs Reorganization Committee, and political affairs will be handled by the Political Affairs Reorganization Committee, respectively. Peiping, Tianjin, Rehe, and Shanhaiguan are as calm as usual. The Central Government will definitely have a solution in the shortest possible time and will never allow the overall situation in North China to be affected. Commander-in-Chief Chiang is very concerned about North China. After I meet with Chairman Han, I will report Han's suggestions to Commander-in-Chief Chiang by telegram. I will stay in Jinan for about three or four days. After completing my mission, I will return to Peiping.

Han Fu-qu said: The resignation of President Wang and Director Zhang was sudden. I am not yet clear about the truth, so I cannot express any opinion. However, at this time when the country is in trouble, I personally believe that the pillars of the country should not resign hastily, giving the enemy an opportunity. I plan to send a telegram to President Wang, earnestly retaining him and asking him to return to the capital as soon as possible to resume his duties, so as to avoid a situation where no one is responsible at the center. In the past two days, neither Commander-in-Chief Chiang nor Director Zhang have sent telegrams to Jinan. Even if Director Zhang resigns, it will certainly not affect the overall situation in North China. However, at a time when both foreign and domestic troubles are pressing, it is really worrying. (August 9)

The case cannot be sent to Beijing for trial. The Provincial Party Headquarters has sent another telegram to the Central Government requesting it to expedite the transfer. Also, all the staff of this headquarters stated that according to the confidential order No. 11 of the National Government on August 19, military agencies have full authority to handle communist cases. Those who have already been sent to the court must be quickly handed back to the military agencies for handling. Only in the Xiao Xuetai case is there a special transfer to Beijing, designated for trial by the court. The law has lost equality, and the anti-communism agencies are the same as being set up in vain. They requested to resign en masse. Furthermore, the division commanders Wang Dongyuan and others jointly sent telegrams urging that if it is not quickly handled according to the law, it will affect the future of the anti-communist campaign. It is not a trivial matter. How should it be handled? Please instruct us to follow. Hunan Anti-Communist Commander He Jian, stamped.

Telegram to the Central Government from the Six Division Commanders: To the Nanjing Central Party Headquarters, National Government, Executive Yuan President Wang, Hankou Military Commission Chairman Chiang, Commander-in-Chief He, Changsha Central Committee Member Fang, Committee Member Hong, Chairman He, Commander-in-Chief He, Anti-Communist Commander He: The Ning case has occurred for a long time, and the hesitation in resolving it has caused alarm far and wide. We believe that the Communist Party is rampant and poisonous, and the whole country is in turmoil. They unscrupulously resort to the schemes of demons and goblins and are accustomed to taking advantage of loopholes. A slight oversight will fall into their trap. Hidden dangers will grow and endanger the foundation of the country. Now, the chief culprit in the Ning case, Xiao Xuetai, and others, have had their evidence published by the Hunan Anti-Communist Command, and the charges are clear. The country has established laws; how can they be allowed to escape cunningly? We are ordered to suppress the reds, and our responsibilities are important. Our subordinates are all requesting, and the public is indignant. We dare to telegraph, asking for a decisive decision, and approve the on-site execution of the criminals according to the law, in order to comfort the sacrificed martyrs and encourage the determination to eliminate communism. We are sincerely requesting and beg for your consideration. Division Commander of the 15th Division Wang Dongyuan, Division Commander of the 10th Division Peng Weiren, Division Commander of the 19th Division Li Jue, Division Commander of the 62nd Division Tao Guang, Division Commander of the 63rd Division Chen Guangzhong, Division Commander of the 34th Division Chen Quzhen, stamped. (August 6)

Continued Interrogation in the Niu Lan Case (Continued) 76

Niu Lan Displays Cunning, Obstinacy, and Evades Questions (Extensive) Money is something everyone has; having money is not in itself harmful to the Republic of China. There is still much evidence, including a proposal from February 10, 1931, according to the Western calendar. The content of the proposal suggests that it is based on reports from the Communist Parties of Hunan, Hubei, and Anhui, and is a recommendation to the central organ of the Communist Party. It states that the party and its Fourth Army Independent Division plan to establish Soviet sub-districts in the southwest of Anhui and the northeast of Hubei, train the Red Army and peasant activists, and suppress the White Army (referring to the Chinese Kuomintang army). The next paragraph also states that before this task is completed, the Red Army should not advance towards the Pinghan Railway Line. Furthermore, there are details on how to mobilize and organize the Red Army, incite workers and peasants near the railway, provoke class struggle, and create red terror, etc. There is also another proposal, which is quite lengthy, recorded on pages 131 to 137 of Volume 2 of the case exhibits." At this point, the original document was handed to Niu for review. After reviewing it, Niu said, "There are ink marks on this document. What is the expert's opinion on this handwriting?" (Presiding Judge:) "We are studying the content first." (Niu:) "I now demand that the expert's opinion be presented. If it is not, it constitutes a rejection of the defendant." (Presiding Judge:) "This document has not been authenticated yet." (Niu:) "The indictment states that I wrote it. I ask the court to present the expert's opinion." (Presiding Judge:) "This exhibit has several points: (1) It mentions dispatching a special comrade to Nanking to contact soldiers and mechanics in the Aviation Administration, and alienate and entice them to disobey central command; (2) At the Shanghai Arsenal, small teams must be organized, with young party members as core members; (3) Regarding the newly organized troops and guards of Chiang Kai-shek, assign ten to fifteen comrades to contact them, and simultaneously expand the Nanking team. Another task is to instigate military rebellion. Furthermore, there is a letter from the Hubei Eastern District Special Committee to you, stating that the Red Army's military actions are slow, and a decision has been made to use part of the army to fight the enemy and another part to create chaos." At this point, Niu requested the court to note that this document was sent from Hubei and typed, but now has ink writing on it, and asked for it to be authenticated. Niu also claimed that none of the letters were signed. (Presiding Judge:) "There is also evidence: a letter from the Central Bureau to the Central District. The letter states that the Seventh and Twentieth Armies in Jiangxi are victorious, but lack 'frames'; send some over. What does this mean?" (Niu:) "This document is unsigned, like the other documents." (Presiding Judge:) "What are 'frames'? Are they people, or weapons?" Niu did not answer. At this point, the Presiding Judge added, "There is also evidence: a letter to the Eastern Secretariat of the Comintern, containing phrases like 'Overthrow Chiang Kai-shek's dictatorial policies,' 'Overthrow the Provisional Constitution,' and 'Overthrow the bandit suppression propaganda.' There is also evidence of the Revolutionary Workers' Union's activities in North China. The original text is very long, and the content involves using practical methods to denounce the Kuomintang as counter-revolutionary, with the most prominent figures being leftist Wang Jingwei and Chen Gongbo, etc. Furthermore, there is the May Day Labor Day Announcement from the Pacific Labor Conference. This announcement is not only in China; Japan, India, Taiwan, and the Philippines all have it. The resolution regarding China includes inciting a revolutionary storm, and Section 4 of it even mentions occupying Chinese territory or part of it. Is this kind of action harmful to the Republic of China?" (Niu:) "This document is in Russian. I don't understand it." (Presiding Judge:) "Furthermore, there is the Far Eastern Bureau's resolution from March 18, 1931, a conversation with comrades from March 27, and news about the Seventh Army, etc. Based on the observation of the above-mentioned evidence, whether they are letters received, official documents, or proposals to the Central Party Headquarters, the facts involve how to deploy troops, how to collude with the military, or how to incite workers and peasants. Based on this, it is naturally of a nature that harms the Republic of China. There are still exhibits, some being past events, some being future plans, all of which are important." At this point, the Presiding Judge ordered Niu to step down and summoned Wang Deli Hui. (Presiding Judge:) "Wang Deli Hui, are you Wang Deli Hui? Are you thirty-seven years old this year?" (Wang:) "A month ago, I said I did not want to answer. Today, my attitude remains unchanged." (Wang:) "The court has convened several times, and I have not seen proof that the High Court has jurisdiction. The Shanghai lawyers' association has issued a declaration stating that the High Court has no jurisdiction. I declare that I reserve the right to speak last." (Presiding Judge:) "Who are you? Who is Niu Lan to you? You say Niu Lan is your husband. Do you have a marriage certificate with Niu Lan?" (Presiding Judge:) "I suspect you are not Niu Lan's wife, but a third country sent you to supervise Niu Lan." (Presiding Judge:) "Niu Lan, Wang Deli Hui, it is now twelve o'clock. We will adjourn the questioning for today. We will resume questioning tomorrow at seven o'clock in the morning." (Presiding Judge:) "The record of the hearing on the fifteenth of last month should be read out today." Thereupon, the Clerk of the Court read out the record. The Presiding Judge then announced the adjournment of the court. It was already twelve twenty. On the morning of the eleventh, at eight o'clock, the Jiangsu High Court, in the First Criminal Court of the Jiangning District Court, continued the trial of Niu Lan and his wife for endangering the Republic of China. The judges present were still Presiding Judge Li Mian, Prosecutor Zhu, two judges, one clerk, and defense lawyer Chen Ying. Geneva barrister Feng Jien also attended as an observer. In addition, about twenty representatives from various relevant agencies attended as observers. After the judges took their seats, Niu Lan and his wife were brought to the court. Presiding Judge Li Mian questioned Niu Lan and his wife in turn regarding the circumstances of the questioning and the responses of Niu Lan and his wife, as follows: (Question:) "Niu Lan, there are over seventy pieces of evidence of your crimes seized from the iron box. Yesterday, I only questioned you on a portion of them. You did not answer. You must understand that the Criminal Procedure Law stipulates that a judgment can be made even if you do not answer." (Niu replied:) "The defendant has confessions at the Shanghai Police Department and the court, which can be investigated." (Question:) "The police witnesses have already appeared in court once and have provided evidence of your crimes." (Niu replied:) "The police record cannot be used as a basis. According to Article 152 of the Criminal Procedure Law, the evidence must be examined in the presence of the defendant. If not in the presence, there must be three witnesses to prove it. Now, relying solely on the police's unilateral evidence is illegal." (Question:) "When the iron box was searched and sent to the police department for inspection at No. 49 Nanjing Road, you were present. The police have already testified to that." (Niu replied:) "According to Article 155 of the Criminal Procedure Law, when examining evidence, the date, location, and details should be listed clearly to serve as a factual basis. The people present should sign the list so that it is valid. The items considered as evidence in this case should also have a list provided to the defendant for review." (Question:) "There is a list, but you do not answer. Why give it to you for review?" (Niu replied:) "The defendant is not proficient in Chinese. Please translate the list into English for verification." (Question:) "The Chinese court should primarily use Chinese. If there is anything unclear, a translator can be used to convey it." (Niu replied:) "If an English list cannot be provided, it proves that the court does not want to make the evidence public." (Question:) "There are three envelopes in the iron box, containing $823 US dollars and $50 Japanese yen. Were these intended to support the Chinese Red Army?" (Niu did not answer.) (Question:) "The witnesses interrogated on the 15th of this month will prove all your evidence at that time." (Niu replied:) "The police department cannot prove anything in this case." (Question:) "The police department is the agency responsible for executing arrest warrants. All the evidence was seized by the police department. Why can't it be proven?" (Niu replied:) "The Shanghai court agreement does not stipulate that the police department can arbitrarily take away the defendant's belongings without providing a clear list for the defendant to review." (Question:) "What exactly did you do in Shanghai?" (Question:) "You said in the High Court that you were doing business. You didn't answer yesterday. Will you answer today?" (Question:) "We will listen to you even if you don't answer, but we still have to ask." (Question:) "Was the deposit slip for seven banks found at No. 74 West Garden, Yu Yuan Road, yours?" (Niu replied:) "Please present the list for me to see." (Question:) "Is it 4,000 yuan deposited in the Yien Yieh Commercial Bank, and 9,000 yuan deposited in the Continental Bank? The deposit in the Yien Yieh Commercial Bank is under the name Xu Weilan." (Niu replied:) "I want to see the list." (Question:) "The list shows 9,000 yuan in the Continental Bank under the name Zhao Cunkai, and 4,000 yuan in the Sze Ming Bank under the name Zhou Jingfu, deposit certificate number 6889, 10,000 yuan in the Bank of China, including 5,000 yuan in Wang Xiaoqin's certificate and 3,000 yuan in Zheng Situi's certificate, 10,000 yuan in the Bank of Communications, deposit certificate number 1579, 7,000 yuan in the China South Bank, originally 9,000 yuan, but 2,000 yuan has been withdrawn by the person himself, and 2,500 yuan in the Day and Night Bank." (Question:) "What is the purpose of depositing money under Chinese names? Is all this money yours?" (Niu replied:) "This was found at No. 74 West Garden, Yu Yuan Road. Please note this in the record." (Question:) "It was found at No. 66 Hart Road. Not No. 74 West Garden. Did you hear clearly? It was found at No. 66 Hart Road." (Niu replied:) "Please note which part of No. 66 the deposit was found in." (Question:) "Is the money yours?" (Niu replied:) "Please provide the search list for No. 66." (Question:) "During the search, you refused to even say your name. How would you sign the list?" (Niu replied:) "Please record that there was no list for the search at No. 66." (Question:) "Another $1,500 US dollars was withdrawn from the Mei Feng Bank by lawyer William on your written instructions. Is this also yours?" (Niu replied:) "Please present the deposit slips from the Bank of China, etc." (Question:) "Just say whether the money is yours or not. Except for the Day and Night Bank, which has ceased operations, the other banks have replied that they have suspended payments." (Niu replied:) "On September 7th last year, the Chinese government published photos of bank deposit slips in newspapers. Now the defendant requests to see the account books, but it is impossible to obtain them. Please take note of this." (Question:) "That is a matter for the administrative authorities." (Question:) "You only need to say whether the money is yours or not." (Niu replied:) "I would like to request the managers of the banks to testify. I have never confronted the bank managers before." (Question:) "What benefit is there to you in requesting the deposit slips?" (Niu replied:) "The defendant has the right to view all kinds of evidence. The court refuses. Please note this in the record." (Question:) "If there is a benefit to you, state the reason, and the deposit slips can be given to you for review." (Niu replied:) "According to Article 284 of the Criminal Procedure Law, the defendant has the right to view them." (Question:) "Article 284 stipulates that the court may allow the defendant to view them, but it does not mean that the defendant can do so freely." (Niu replied:) "The defendant has the right to view the bank deposit certificates." (Question:) "The banks all have replies that can substitute for the deposit slips." (Niu replied:) "Please record that there are no deposit slips." (Question:) "Do you want to see the name and seals? You have more than a dozen aliases." (Niu replied:) "The iron [cabinet] at [Hart Road] No. 66, I request to be sent down for inspection." (Question:) "Your name can be changed at any time. The court believes that

it is not necessary to show it to you." At this point, the judge listed the names Niu had changed. (Niu replied:) "Why could you show me those three boxes yesterday, but you can't show me

the iron cabinet today?" (Question:) "This iron cabinet has not been sent over yet. When it is sent over, it will not matter if you see it or not. Just say if the money is yours or not." (Niu replied:) "Record that this cabinet was taken to the police department." (Question:) "Regarding this point, the witnesses on the 15th will prove it." (Question:) "The US dollars were withdrawn by the lawyer on your written instructions. It is all yours, isn't it?" (Niu replied:) "There are two letters for the withdrawal of money from Mei Feng." (Question:) "Did you write the letters?" (Niu replied:) "Please note a few points: (1) The applications from the Shanghai banks; (2) Mei Feng Bank was summoned for questioning; (3) I was taken to Mei Feng, and Mei Feng acknowledged that I was Heyers; (4) At that time, Mei Feng acknowledged that I, Heyers, lived at No. 66 Hart Road." (Question:) "Zhu Yousong from Mei Feng has testified, and he said it very clearly." (Question:) "You are a teacher. Why do you have eight mailboxes rented at the post office? (1) No. 206; (2) No. 1265; (3) No. 1518; (4) No. 1382; (5) No. 1077; (6) No. 1085; (7) No. 883; (8) No. 1532. What did you rent these mailboxes for?" (Niu replied:) "Now I

request that Mailbox No. 206 and the communist evidence inside be presented for my review." (Question:) "First, we ask if the mailbox is yours." (Niu replied:) "The Supreme Court's investigation has already shown it to me." (Question:) "Even if we bring Mailbox No. 106, you will say it is not yours." (Niu replied:) "Please record that there is only one mailbox, No. 206. There are no others." (Question:) "You are deliberately making trouble. Even if we put all the boxes here, you might still say they are not yours." (Niu replied:) "Please note that the indictment is for Heyers, and the application is for Niu Lan." (Question:) "We will resolve the eight mailboxes one by one. Answer the first one first. Just say if No. 206 is yours or not." (Niu replied:) "There is more to say." (Question:) "First, say if the first mailbox is yours or not." (Niu replied:) "If the court uses coercion, I will not speak." (Question:) "Asking if Mailbox No. 206 is yours, how is that coercion?" (Niu replied:) "The court is violating Article 284 of the Criminal Procedure Law." (Question:) "You are deliberately disrupting things. What is the meaning of this?" (To be continued.)

Wu Qiwel's Troops Suppress Bandit Lairs in the Gan River Area 77

The Wu Division Arrives in Ji'an and Contacts Various Armies. Nanchang Correspondence: After Zhang Fakui's Fourth Army moved from Guangxi Province to Qingjiang, Zhangshu, Xingan, and Gaoan, it was ordered to be reduced to the Ninetieth Division, with Wu Qiwel serving as the Division Commander and Deputy Army Commander. They were ordered to concentrate in Ji'an from Zhangshu, responsible for attacking the bandit lairs on the east bank of the Gan River. According to news from Ji'an, Wu Qiwel led all his troops to Ji'an and contacted Wei Zhuoying's troops to actively suppress scattered bandits near Ji'an, Jishui, and Taihe. They are preparing to take Futian via Shuinan, Yangtian, and Luojiawei, and then directly attack Donggu to assault Xingguo. At the same time, the troops of Gao Shuxun, Li Kunsong, Xu Kexiang, Mao Bingwen, and Li Yunjie in central and eastern Gan are also actively advancing south. Mao's troops have passed Ganzhu and are only thirty to forty li away from the county seat of Guangchang. Gao's troops have defeated the pseudo-Fourth and Fifth Independent Divisions in Zhongsha, Dongpi, and Luofang, and destroyed the pseudo-Farmers' Association and pseudo-Soviet agencies, as well as the memorial halls of Marx and Lenin. They are preparing to clear the scattered bandits there and then join Mao's troops to attack Huangpi, Xiaopu, and Luokou in Ningdu to recover Ningdu, and then join Wu's troops in Yudu, with the aim of suppressing all bandit lairs in the Gan River area. (August 8)

Hu Zongnan's Division Returns to Anqing to Await Orders 78

The Bandit Suppression in Western Anhui Comes to an End. Anqing Correspondence: Hu Zongnan, the commander of the First Division, recently received orders to lead his troops to suppress Red bandits in the counties of Lu'an, Shucheng, Yingshan, and Huoshan, with considerable success. The division has now received orders to return to the province. The vanguard of the Second Brigade, Yuan Pu's troops, arrived in the province a few days ago. Hu continued to arrive in the province on the afternoon of the ninth. The division headquarters is located in the Longmenkou Senior High School. The troops of the First Brigade are also arriving in the province one after another to await orders. According to Hu's account of the bandit suppression, the division went to western Anhui in June and has been suppressing bandits for more than two months. After three general offensives, the bandits retreated to the west of the Piji River. The division learned that the people in Shucheng and Liuhuo have been exploited and oppressed by corrupt local bullies and are in dire straits. Therefore, the division, together with the local county government, severely punished the corrupt local bullies. At the same time, it organized relief work in the disaster areas, so the division received assistance from the people wherever it went. The Liuhuo area is rich in tea and forest resources, exceeding the entire province. Since the blockade of the bandit areas, goods have been unable to be transported out, and resources are worthless. There are countless people nearby who lack food and clothing. After the recovery, the displaced people will gradually gather and will be able to work hard to produce and improve people's livelihoods. I stayed in Sanwanghe Village near Huoshan for a long time. The village's herdboy are very smart and lovely, so I established a special class for herdboy in the people's school established by the division and encouraged them to enroll. (August 11)

Conflict Between the Red Flag Society and the Black Flag Society in Southern Shandong 79

Many Casualties on Both Sides

The Garrison Troops Exert Efforts to Suppress the Situation

Jinan Correspondence: Secret societies in southern Shandong have been prevalent. In the early days of organization, villagers joined each other for mutual assistance. Over time, cunning people took advantage of it to build their personal power, and conflicts often occurred due to conflicts of interest. This spring, a dispute arose between the Black Flag Society of Yishui and the district chief, resulting in a major disturbance. The district chief died, and several members of the militia and the society were killed or injured. Fortunately, the Director of Civil Affairs, Li Shuchun, went to Yishui to console the people and restore peace. Just a few months later, the Red Flag Society and the Black Flag Society in Yishui and Ju County clashed again due to minor matters, and the disturbance is becoming increasingly serious. There is a village called Gaojiazhuang in Yishui, which is within the scope of the Red Flag Society, and they have deep animosity towards the Black Flag Society. One day, some Black Flag Society members gathered to gamble in Gaojiazhuang, and were dispersed and insulted by members of the Red Flag Society. The Black Flag Society held a grudge and gathered two thousand members, led by their leader Sun, to attack Dongjiagou ten days ago. Dongjiagou is within the scope of the Red Flag Society, and they were caught off guard. More than eighty people were outnumbered, and either died, were injured, or escaped. Since then, the resentment has deepened, and the Red Flag Society members vowed to retaliate. Therefore, the Black Flag Society members took the initiative and mobilized thousands of members to suddenly attack Mantangpo, the Red Flag Society's base, on July 27 (twenty-five li southeast of Yishui, fifty-five li northwest of Ju County). The Red Flag Society happened to be gathering there for discussions and had prepared early. They immediately opened fire, and the sound of gunfire shook the surrounding area. The Red Flag Society was ultimately outnumbered and unable to break through. However, more than seventy Black Flag Society members were killed or injured while trying to climb the walls at night. The incident occurred near Ju County and Yishui. Therefore, the county heads of both counties, fearing that the disturbance would expand further and lead to a major change, reported to the provincial government and the Department of Civil Affairs, and sent personnel to mediate, urging both sides to stop the attack in order to discuss a settlement. Yishui was originally garrisoned by a regiment of the Yunqi Brigade of the Eighty-first Division. After the incident, they are suppressing the situation there. If the disturbance expands further, more troops may be dispatched. At the same time as the conflict between the Black Flag Society and the Red Flag Society in Yishui, there was also news of a conflict between the Yellow Flag Society members of Zhucheng and the garrison troops. It is reported that a battalion of the Rong Guangxing unit of the Eighty-seventh Brigade of the Twenty-ninth Division is stationed there. A soldier was injured by the Yellow Flag Society members a few days ago. The soldiers were furious and opened fire. Fortunately, local gentry and Battalion Commander Dang intervened and mediated, and the situation has now completely calmed down. (August 8)

Bandits Captured on the Jing-Wu Steamer 80

A Total of Five Box Cannons Seized

Wuhu Correspondence: Small steamers traveling to various places from Wuhu have been robbed an unknown number of times. After the Training Corps of the Central Military Academy was stationed in Wuhu, it dispatched troops to escort the steamers on the Jing-Wu, Hefei, Chaoxian, and Datong routes and strictly inspected the docks in various ports, and the bandits began to restrain themselves somewhat. At the same time, the detective team of the Public Security Bureau and the military police inspection station of the Training Corps also worked hard to investigate and successively solved the robbery cases on the Datong and Jing-Wu steamers, capturing many bandits and firearms. However, yesterday, the Hengfu merchant steamer, which had been robbed not long ago and was traveling between Nanking and Wuhu, was sailing from Jing to Wu. When it reached Dashengguan, thirty li from Jing, it stopped as usual. Two rowboats carried more than twenty passengers to the small steamer. The escorting soldiers conducted inspections according to law. Unexpectedly, six of them, Zhou Lianqing, Pan Chongyi, Tang Ximing, Gong Zhenhui, and Peng Yunsheng, speaking with a Guangxi accent, refused to be inspected, claiming that they had official business to Woyang County to arrest bandits. Zhang Chenghai, the company commander of the Training Corps escorting the steamer, found their movements suspicious and searched them in detail. Four box cannons and one Browning pistol were found on their waists and legs. At that time, the bandits resisted slightly, causing Huang Chuanshou, the platoon leader of the escorting troops, to be injured in the hand. However, due to the bravery of the soldiers, the bandits were successively subdued and escorted to Wuhu, and then transferred to the Training Corps headquarters for interrogation. At that time, a rice merchant on the steamer, named Jia, was carrying four or five thousand yuan in cash. After the bandits were captured, Jia was extremely grateful and offered some money to thank the soldiers of the Training Corps. The team believed that it was their duty to escort the steamer and capture bandits, and declined the offer. (August 9)

Hand Grenade Explosion Injures People in Bangbu 81

Six People Injured, Young Girl in Critical Condition. Bangbu Correspondence: On the afternoon of the ninth, at six o'clock, the mortar company of the Sixty-eighth Regiment of Ma Kun's Thirty-fourth Brigade of the Twelfth Division, stationed in Bangbu, hired three carts full of hand grenades to transport them from the Far East Apartment to the opposite side of Tongfeng Sesame Cake Factory on Jing [Road], intending to transport them to Hefei the next day. While passing through the Yixingyong Cloth Store in the third section of Zhongzheng Street in the city, due to the hot weather, the hand grenades on the last cart were shaken and rubbed against each other, and three of them suddenly exploded with three loud bangs. The glass doors and windows of the Yixingyong store were immediately shattered. Pedestrians did not know the truth and fled in panic. The carts were also destroyed in the explosion, and six men and women were injured. After investigation, the injured included rickshaw puller Zhao Xiling, who was injured in the head and feet, and the wife of Xi Xingzhi, the owner of the Yixingyong Cloth Store, Xi Shao, who was holding her one-year-old granddaughter, Xiao Congzi, in her arms, idly looking at the street. Xi Shao was injured in the head, and her granddaughter was injured in three places on her legs, with two toes blown off. She was seriously injured and may die. At that time, a passerby, Shao Liangchen, was injured in the head and feet. Guo Yin, the wife of Guo Dingguo, was passing by and was slightly injured in the leg. Police Officer Wang Qiming was slightly injured in the right leg by a shrapnel shard, but it was not serious. After the incident, the company commander, Tang Qingchang, immediately sent someone to take rickshaw puller Zhao Xiling to the Twelfth Division's military hospital for treatment. The unexploded hand grenades were still sent to Jing [Road]. Xi Shao and her granddaughter were sent to Pingxin Hospital on Damalu by their family members for treatment. Shao Liangchen and Guo Yin were sent to Wenfang Hospital on Ermalu by the police. Zhang Guanru, the director of the Third Branch of the Public Security Bureau, dispatched police to investigate the incident within his jurisdiction after the hand grenade explosion and reported it to the headquarters. After receiving the report, You Kaiyun, the director of the Public Security Bureau, sent personnel to visit the injured in various hospitals and reported the truth of the case to Jiang Dingwen, the commander of the garrison headquarters. In the past two months, there have been two other tragic bombing incidents in Bangbu. This is the third time. (August 9)

Local Correspondence

Suzhou 82

Old Painter Entices and Rapes Young Girls: Ni Xiaojun, an old pencil painter of sixty-two years, though old in age, commits all kinds of evil. He specializes in enticing poor girls of only ten years and older, committing rape, and then forcing them into prostitution to enrich himself. It is said that he has as many as fifty or sixty "adopted daughters." Moreover, he is skilled in the art of "collecting yin to nourish yang," so although he is old, his spirit is very strong. Gu Zixuan's thirteen-year-old daughter was also enticed, raped, and forced into prostitution. It was reported to the Public Security Bureau, and Ni was arrested. After a preliminary interrogation by the Judicial Section, he was escorted to court for trial yesterday (the 11th) afternoon.

Money Shop Clerk Defrauds Huge Sums: The Jin Feng Money Shop in Tongli Town, Wujiang County, is quite large in scale and has dealings with various money shops in Suzhou, enjoying considerable credit. Wang and Li, the internal and external clerks of the shop, recently stole the shop's seals. Wang came to Suzhou and used written requests to borrow 5,000 yuan in paper money from each of the Fu Da, Bao Da, Feng Tai, Jiu Yuan, and Yi Cheng Yu shops. The Fu Da, Bao Da, Feng Tai, and Jiu Yuan shops did not suspect anything and paid the full amount. However, Yi Cheng Yu did not have such a large amount of paper money at the time, so it was not delivered. A few hours later, someone was sent to deliver it to the Suzhou Tongban Steamboat, but the steamboat had already departed, so it was taken back. The next day (the 10th), Jin Feng Shop sent someone to Suzhou to settle the account with Feng Tai. Gu Xing learned of the previous situation and immediately reported it to the shop via long-distance telephone. Pang Baisheng, the manager of the shop, immediately came to Suzhou by boat to search for Wang and Li, but they were nowhere to be found.

Anti-Japanese Association Executive Arrested: The Wu County Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association has been working hard since the Shanghai Incident, sparing no effort in inspecting Japanese goods. Recently, rumors have been circulating that the association has colluded with unscrupulous merchants to smuggle Japanese goods. The matter came to the attention of the county party headquarters, which sent personnel to take away the association's documents for review. Provincial party headquarters sent Lu Baolin to Suzhou to investigate the case against the county party headquarters and took the opportunity to investigate the Anti-Japanese Association case. He believed that the Anti-Japanese Association was indeed colluding with unscrupulous merchants, so the party headquarters notified the Public Security Bureau to send personnel to arrest Huang Zixin, the executive of the Anti-Japanese Association, who is being temporarily detained at the Public Security Bureau pending interrogation. It is said that the association has confiscated Japanese goods worth over 20,000 yuan, which will soon be auctioned off.

Kunshan 83

Provincial Water Police Capture Thieves in Dian Shan Lake: Ge Xiancai, captain of the 12th Provincial Public Security Water Police Team stationed in Kunshan, was ordered to suppress bandits. He immediately led six naval vessels to patrol Dian Shan Lake. At about 11 p.m. the night before, Captain Ge saw a bandit ship passing by in the lake and immediately ordered gunfire. The bandits returned fire. After fifteen minutes, the bandits could not hold out and retreated. Captain Ge pursued and captured the bandits Xu Decai, Yu Yanxiaoyue, and Hua Xiang on the spot, seizing three rifles and two bandit ships. On the 10th, he took the team to interrogate the bandits, who all confessed to being bandit boatmen. They were immediately detained pending transfer to the district headquarters for disposal.

Kidnappers Release Hostages: The families of Wang Hanchen and Zhou Zhiren in Pingzhuangdian, Baicheng, were robbed by bandits some time ago, and Zhou Zhiren and Wang's son and daughter-in-law were kidnapped. It has been three months. The day before yesterday, Quan Lin, a detective stationed in Shanghai by the County Public Security Bureau, arrested eight bandits, including Zhou Xiaomazi, in Shanghai. They were sent to Kunshan for interrogation. They later confessed to the location where the hostages were held. The county government is trying to rescue them. The hostages suddenly returned home on the 11th, but Zhou Zhiren got lost in Shanghai due to unfamiliarity with the route. The Zhou family has now sent people to Shanghai to search for him.

Wuxi 84

Qualified Teachers Strive for Better Treatment: The recently stipulated qualifications for teachers in this county must be re-certified after five years. It is believed that education is constantly changing, and teachers should also evolve with the times to adapt to the environment. However, graduates of normal high schools believe that they have the qualifications of natural teachers and do not need to be re-certified. However, no one can guarantee whether these graduates can evolve with the times and adapt to the environment. Therefore, the Department of Education's regulations are somewhat favorable to graduates and unfavorable to qualified teachers. Therefore, the qualified teachers have requested the Education Association to submit a report to the department to appeal. This was passed by the association's third representative congress and was submitted to the Department of Education for review yesterday.

Borrowing Money to Irrigate Yellowing and Dying Rice: This county has been suffering from a prolonged drought with no rain, and a drought has already formed. Yesterday, someone came to the city from Beiqiao in the west countryside. Along the way, only four mu of rice fields had a little water. The rest were dry and cracked, and some fields had yellowed and died. Farmers do not have enough food to eat, so how can they have the surplus to irrigate? Yuan Fengqi, the district chief of the tenth district, etc., in order to seek irrigation, specially negotiated with the Farmers Bank to borrow 3,000 yuan, with a monthly interest rate of 1.2%, specifically for farmers to irrigate their fields. Each household is limited to 40 yuan, and oil is paid instead of silver. However, only farmers with guaranteed credit have the right to borrow money. Sha Kunquan, a resident of the seventeenth district, also borrowed money from the Farmers Bank on behalf of the farmers to provide irrigation.

Changzhou 85

Red Spear Society Suspects Arrested: Zhu Sen, a patrol officer in Cuiqiao, the sixth district of Wu County, received a report on the morning of the 10th that a boat had arrived in the town with four passengers whose whereabouts were suspicious, fearing that they were not good people. Patrol Officer Zhu immediately joined forces with the security corps to surround and arrest them, capturing Chen Shoukang, Wang Yaochu, Xu Meida, and Yun Zixiang, and seizing a Red Spear Society scripture, two talismans, and name cards for the Big Sword Team. After a preliminary trial, the suspects confessed to borrowing guns from friends for robbery and revenge. The suspects were sent to the Public Security Bureau for transfer to the county government for trial.

County Government Strictly Pursues Overdue Grain Tax: The Wu County Money and Grain Tax Review Committee recently found that Zhao Yiguan in Fangxiang owed the most grain tax in the city and countryside, amounting to 1,200 to 300 yuan. Zhao Yiguan was ordered to appear in court for questioning and detention. The court hearing was held on the afternoon of the 10th, and he was given seven days to pay half of the amount before being released on bail. Others who have not paid are being arrested by name.

Rugao 86

County Relief Branch Cables Province to Report Disaster: The county relief branch yesterday sent a cable to the provincial relief association stating, "This county suffered a severe flood last year, causing great damage and deep pain, which has not yet recovered. Since the beginning of summer this year, there has been no rain for more than a month, the river has dried up, the seedlings have withered, and the drought has become apparent. Looking to the future, we are deeply afraid. In addition to submitting a report on the disaster situation in succession, we should first submit a respectful cable report."

Gaoyou 87

Bandit Robbery Causes One Death: Qin Dayou, a farmer from the northern countryside of this county, came to the city for business the other day and returned home in the afternoon. When passing near Mapeng Bay, he suddenly encountered two bandits, each holding firearms, who twisted Qin and searched his body. They only found five silver dollars. At that time, a passerby happened to pass by, and the bandits were quite alarmed, so they opened fire and shot at the passerby. The bullet hit a vital part, and he fell to the ground and died on the spot. It was truly tragic.

Bandits Loot Yongfeng Town: Yongfeng Town, under the jurisdiction of Baoying County, is adjacent to Gaoyou and Yizheng counties. Early in the morning the other day, more than 400 bandits suddenly poured in from Yizheng County. Most of them were wearing gray military uniforms and had complete firearms. They looted the town, kidnapped more than 60 men and women, and shot several townspeople. The bandits are still entrenched near the town. The townspeople have now sent representatives to the Baoying County Government to report and request that a team be sent to suppress them immediately.

Nantong 88

Issuing County Surtax Promissory Notes: The Nantong County surtax revenue for past years is at 70%. The property management office maintains the status quo and relies solely on saving money. The accumulated deficit has reached more than 170,000 yuan. The local tax revenue for the 20th year is less than 50%, and the shortfall is even greater. In order to alleviate the emergency, the county government submitted a request to the county administrative meeting to issue Nantong County surtax promissory notes in imitation of the provincial method, using local surtaxes as collateral. It was decided on the 10th that the total amount would be from 100,000 to 150,000 yuan, with face values of one yuan, five yuan, and ten yuan. The county government, the finance bureau, and the property management office will jointly handle it.

The Poison of Opium and Red Pills is Deepening: Nantong has always been an opium market in Jiangbei. Recently, local vendors have been openly active, opium prohibition has been relaxed, and the market for red pills is even wider. According to investigations, the recent increase in the number of opium users is extremely alarming.

Yangzhou 89

Three More Cases of Robbery and Kidnapping: Robbery cases have occurred frequently in the four districts of Jiangdu. The county bureau's arresting officers are almost exhausted. The home of Chen Beiluan in Hui Maojian, the first village of Huanghualing in the seventh district, was also invaded by more than ten bandits before dawn on the 9th. They rummaged through boxes and cabinets, searching for valuables. When the three squads of the security corps in the district heard the alarm and rushed there, the bandits fled towards Ailing Lake. At 8 p.m. the same afternoon, the home of a Yuan family resident of Huaizi Bridge outside the north gate was also attacked by eight bandits with boxes, pistols, and handguns. They broke into the house and kidnapped their eight-year-old son. On the morning of the 10th, the families of Lu Neisen and Lu Guojiu in Xinghuawei Village, Kongjia Bridge, were robbed one after another by dozens of bandits. They also forced Lu Guojiu to write a note for 2,000 yuan, limited to five days, to be delivered to the south end of Guangfu Bridge in Yiling. They rushed to report to the county government and requested an investigation.

Chamber of Commerce Bails Out Bandit Suspect Detective: Hu Keyin, a detective of the Public Security Detective Team, was previously accused of colluding with bandits by Yang Suxiang, a detective of the same team. He was detained and sent to the county detective team for questioning. Yang, the county magistrate, accepted the request of Wang Jingting, chairman of the Chamber of Commerce, and Dai Jingshan, a standing committee member, and approved the Chamber of Commerce to bail him out. Hu was ordered to return to the team to serve and work hard to redeem himself. He was released on bail at 3 p.m. on the 9th.

Bandits Rob and Kidnap: The home of Yuan Zhengui, the owner of the Yuan Shunxing pig shop in Wangjiaxiang, the eastern and western Wan villages in the northern countryside of the county, was suddenly attacked by more than ten bandits at 7 p.m. the other day (the 8th). They held handguns and shouted to prevent any noise. They first tied up Yuan's wife, Wang, and forced her to hand over money. Then they injured Yuan's son, Youyu, and his daughter-in-law, Yang, and robbed the shop's self-defense gun with sixty rounds of ammunition, as well as a large number of silver dollars and jewelry. They also kidnapped Yuan's grandson, Yonghao (14 years old). Before leaving, they fired a shot to show their strength and fled by boat to Chenjiagou.

Shaobo Rice Donation Solicitation: The Bureau of Education considers that the rice donation in Bobo was previously collected by merchants in that area on a seasonal basis. However, the collection has been sluggish, and there are many arrears. Now, it is changed to soliciting bids from merchants for the annual donation, with the minimum amount being 270 yuan per year. The bidding will be held at the county government at 10 a.m. on the 20th of this month.

Jiading 90

Old Woman Commits Suicide by Jumping into Well Due to Poverty and Illness: An old Cao woman living in the city's Xueqiao Tui has one son who married into a family outside the south gate and one daughter who married into a barber shop on East Main Street a month ago. The old woman has no support and is suffering from poverty and illness, moaning in bed for half a month. Feeling pitiful for her situation, she suddenly had a suicidal thought. On the 8th, when no one was prepared, she went downstairs alone and secretly committed suicide by jumping into a well. By the time passersby discovered her and rescued her, she had already died.

Xiaoshan 91

Soldier Falls to Death from Car While Picking Up Hat: On the morning of the 8th, a bus on the Xiaoshan Highway had a security team soldier, Xu Xisheng, traveling from Xiguo to Jiangbian. When near Qianqing, his military hat was suddenly blown off by the wind. The soldier immediately jumped out of the car to pick up the hat, seriously injuring himself and falling to the ground. The car stopped immediately, and the wounded soldier was carried onto the car and driven to Xiaoshan Station, intending to send him to Xiaoshan Hospital for treatment. However, he was fatally injured and died on the spot. The military officer reported it to the county court for an autopsy and provided a coffin.

Large Number of Prisoners Released in Recent Days: The Xiaoshan County Court released a large number of prisoners on parole by provincial order. Eleven people were released on the 7th, and more than 20 others will be released in succession. The prison wardens are ordered to clean up the prison cells.

Letter Received

Letter from Qidong County Government 92

Respectfully, regarding the report in the Nantong communications column of your newspaper on August 6th about the Qidong bandit rebellion requesting assistance, this is inconsistent with the facts. Since September of last year, there have been no pirate robberies or Red Bandit disturbances in this county. The dispatch of troops to Qidong was ordered by the Qin Military Commission and the Provincial Security Office, and not because this government requested assistance due to a bandit rebellion. Fearing that the rumors are untrue, we hereby send a special letter of clarification, respectfully requesting that your newspaper publish it in the local communications column to set the record straight. Fei Gongxia, August 9th.

Educational News

Special Feature

Thoughts on the National Sports Conference 93

By Lu Peixuan (1) 94

Physical education occupies an important position in education. It is also an essential element for preserving the nation and solving the people's livelihood. Therefore, those who advocate education to save the country and the Three Principles of the People to govern the country must not regard physical education as insignificant. In the past, physical education focused on developing the body and mind, emphasizing health but neglecting the development of individuality. Today's physical education only values competition skills, paying little attention to basic training. As a result, the health of the body and mind and the presence or absence of defects are completely ignored. Society often despises athletes, believing that their character is often crude and their studies are often poor. This is a case of throwing out the baby with the bathwater. Alas, physical education, physical education, all sins can be masked in your name. Is this the fault of physical education? No, it is due to a lack of systematic organization, a lack of good teachers to train physical education, and a lack of understanding of the true meaning and purpose of physical education. Now, the Ministry of Education is convening a national sports conference, bringing together national sports experts and relevant personnel to define a physical education program and solve various problems in physical education. This move is a new record in our country's history. The future of physical education is bright and promising. However, I have some contributions to make: this conference should widely gather talents, and special attention should be paid to children's physical education to lay a foundation. Do not entrust it to those with no experience in elementary school physical education. Therefore, regardless of whether they are experts in large, medium, or small schools, men or women, they should all be convened. The mission of this conference is to preserve the vitality of the nation, assist in the development of the people's livelihood, and promote the development of education. It is not a regular conference that can be perfunctorily handled. Now, I will try to propose seventeen motions below for public discussion, hoping that my comrades will advance and teach them. (1) Popularize the Spirit of Gentleman Athletes: The term "Sportsmanship" has been translated by some as the benevolent and chivalrous spirit in sports. I think it should be simply called "Gentleman Athlete," and loyalty, filial piety, benevolence, love, trustworthiness, righteousness, and peace should be the necessary conditions for a gentleman athlete. Let me break it down as follows: (A) Loyalty and Filial Piety: Loyalty to the nation, loyalty to the motherland, loyalty to the alma mater, group duties, | fulfilling responsibilities | respecting teachers | mutual assistance.

(B) Benevolence and Love: Do not do to others what you do not want done to yourself, | loving the group, loving people, loving yourself, loving things. (C) Trustworthiness and Righteousness: Obeying rules, abiding by conventions, extending to abiding by laws, as well as courage, sacrifice, and obedience. (D) Peace: Physical education without competition has no progress, but competition is a method, not an end. Moreover, if there is no gentlemanly spirit in competition, it is no different from the barbaric touches of wild beasts, not different from being in the ranks of uncivilized people, harming the body and mind, destroying personality, and wasting studies. What is the value of this kind of physical education? Therefore, I must advocate the gentlemanly spirit. The ultimate goal of the Kuomintang is the world commonwealth, and the ideal of physical education is to strive for peace, that is, to compete in the world arena with physique, physical fitness, and physical strength, and gradually expect the physical education of all nations to develop equally in order to maintain peace and abolish all inhumane struggles. This is the highest ideal of physical education. (This article is limited by space and will be discussed in detail later.) According to the development and popularization of foreign physical education, it all depends on this kind of spirit, which is known to almost every household, old and young. Our country urgently needs to popularize it. Starting from senior elementary school, we must start to promote its meaning and practice it at any time. The responsibility should be borne by physical education teachers, and the principal and the personnel of the academic and training departments should inspect and correct it at any time. (2) The National Physical Education Law should be revised as soon as possible. (The National Physical Education Law can be found in the records of the National Education Conference in the 17th year.) This is because the law's content governs the powers of physical education unclearly (there is a reproach of "one monk carries water to drink, two monks carry water to drink, and three monks have no water to drink"), and there are many restrictions and few rewards, which is a loss of the intention to promote it. (3) Zhang Xueliang's proposal for eight physical education programs should be explained and implemented in detail. The plan proposed by Zhang was adopted at the Fourth Plenary Session in the 19th year. The implied meaning is excellent. This conference should formulate implementation methods so as not to lose the reproach of empty words. For example, Article 6 of the original text pays attention to making industrial and commercial circles and civil servants have considerable time to engage in sports outside of their business. How can store managers and factory directors not interfere with the spare time sports of partners and apprentices?

National Sports Conference 97

The Conference will Discuss Two Issues

| Emphasize Sports Administration | | Confirm the Status of National Arts | Wu Yunrui Talked in Shanghai Yesterday

Wu Yunrui, a member of the preparatory committee for the National Sports Conference and a member of the drafting committee for the National Sports Program, came to Shanghai from Beijing yesterday for personal matters. Our reporter specially visited Wu and asked him about the various aspects of the National Sports Conference. Wu replied with the following two important points:

Emphasize Sports Administration: This conference will have precise discussions on sports administration in order to urge promotion. Educational institutions from the Ministry of Education to provinces, cities, and counties will establish sports administrators to supervise the implementation of sports in various places at any time in order to achieve practical promotion.

Confirm the Status of National Arts: Recently, the national arts community has been promoting its cause vigorously. At the same time, there seems to be some conflict with the sports community. However, national arts cannot be called the entire sports, nor is it a matter outside the scope of sports. It is only a part of sports. A status will be determined specifically to promote national arts. The above two points are the essential issues for the sports community in our country. It can also be said to be a method of "administering medicine according to the symptoms." Once implemented in the future, it will be a major plan for the revitalization of the sports community in our country. It is said that Wu will leave Shanghai and return to Beijing at 9 a.m. this morning.

Brief Rules for Member Reception (1) After receiving the order from the Ministry of Education, various institutions and schools should send a letter separately, or report to the Ministry of Education, with the names and resumes of the attendees, so as to compile a list of members. (2) Attending members must bring their credentials and report to the reception section of the Preparatory Committee of the National Sports Conference of the Ministry of Education on Chengxian Street, Nanjing, before August 16th. (3) The following items must be collected when reporting: 1. Admission badges and handbooks for the venue, 2. Draft resolutions and other printed materials that have been sorted and printed, 3. If you need the association to prepare food and accommodation, you can sign to receive the food and accommodation certificate, 4. The agenda for the first general meeting, 5. Other (4) The period for the association to receive members is from August 16th to 21st, a total of six days. Non-members or attendants accompanying members will not be received. (5) The association will designate the bed in the hostel room. After the member confirms it, it cannot be changed. (6) The association will designate the time for members to eat in the dining hall. The regulations are as follows (no waiting after the time): 1. Breakfast at 6:00 a.m. 2. Lunch at 12:00 noon, 3. Dinner at 7:00 p.m. (7) During the meeting period, the association will prepare vehicles for group activities or special needs. No vehicles will be provided for other personal access. (8) Stationery, envelopes, paper, and pens will be provided by the association. Members can collect them from the reception section with a material collection certificate. (9) All pocket money shall be prepared by the members themselves. (10) If a member wants to entrust the association to handle an event, please contact the receptionist. The receptionist may refuse if he considers it difficult. (11) Members must abide by the rules of the club when staying and attending meetings at the Lizhi Society, and smoking and drinking are prohibited. (12) These brief rules shall be implemented after being approved by the preparatory committee and reported to the Ministry of Education for record. (13) If there are any deficiencies or improprieties in these brief rules, the preparatory committee shall revise them at any time.

Beauty Swimmer McKim Placed Fourth in 100m Freestyle 98

Specially permitted attendees must prepare everything at their own expense. Other details are listed in the brief rules for reception.

More than 190 Proposals Divided into 20 Categories: The National Sports Conference will be held at the Lizhi Society at 8:00 a.m. to 10:00 a.m. on the 16th for the opening ceremony. 400-Meter Freestyle 101

Intense Competition Between American, Japanese, and French Swimmers

American Gulub Takes First Place

All Top Six Break Olympic Records (Dentsu, Los Angeles, 10th) The final of today's 100-meter freestyle swimming competition began at 3:30 PM. The three Japanese athletes, Oyakota, Yokoyama, and Sugimoto, departed with an air of determination to win etched on their faces. However, they were ultimately defeated by their strong American and French rivals, finishing in third, fourth, and fifth place, respectively. When Gulub was confirmed in first place and Oyakota in third, the Japanese supporters' section was silent. Only when the three athletes retired did they applaud to console their final efforts. The results are as follows: First: Gulub (USA), 4 minutes 48.4 seconds (New Olympic Record); Second: Darley (France), 4 minutes 48.5 seconds (New Olympic Record);

Third: Tsutomu Oyakota (Japan), 4 minutes 52.3 seconds (New Olympic Record); Fourth: Takashi Yokoyama (Japan), 4 minutes 52.5 seconds (New Olympic Record); Fifth: Sakari Sugimoto (Japan), 4 minutes 56.1 seconds (New Olympic Record); Sixth: Charlton (Australia), 4 minutes 58.9 seconds (New Olympic Record). All six broke the previous Olympic record of 5 minutes 1 second set by Chorila, creating new Olympic records. Today, Japanese expatriates had expected a victory, so the audience was very enthusiastic, but the unexpected defeat was very disappointing. Fortunately, they earned nine points, which is still satisfying. Oyakota, who finished third, was quite thin after his illness and shed tears like rain. When the athletes rested before returning to the pool, he only said "regret, regret." Yokoyama, who finished fourth, told reporters that swimming next to Darley required more effort than he had anticipated. He swam hard throughout but ultimately failed, which was a great regret.

The Course of the 400-Meter Freestyle Final (Dentsu, Los Angeles, 10th) Today’s 400-meter freestyle final, the focus of swimming interest, proceeded as follows: All six started simultaneously, with Darley swimming powerfully and taking the lead, followed by Gulub. Oyakota was in third place, with Sugimoto and Yokoyama slightly behind, swimming shoulder to shoulder. At 50 meters, Darley and Gulub were two meters apart, while Oyakota was already three meters behind, striving to catch up. After Gulub, the order was Charlton, Sugimoto, and Yokoyama, until 100 meters, when Darley was four meters ahead, swimming in the lead. The order remained the same. Upon passing 150 meters, Gulub suddenly surged forward, swimming ahead alone, with Sugimoto and Yokoyama striving to catch up. Charlton lagged behind at the end. At 200 meters, Darley overtook Gulub again. Gulub, four meters behind, chased vigorously, followed by Oyakota, one meter further behind. Sugimoto and Yokoyama were two meters behind. After 250 meters, Darley showed signs of fatigue, and his swimming power greatly decreased. Gulub gradually advanced, striving to close the gap, with Oyakota swimming one meter behind. At 300 meters, Gulub became unstoppable, like a dragon in the water, turning freely. After 350 meters, with only 20 meters to the finish, Gulub caught up with Darley, and they sprinted shoulder to shoulder, initiating a fierce competition. Gulub ultimately reached the finish line first, winning the championship. From first to sixth place, all broke the Olympic record of 5 minutes 1.6 seconds set by Argentine athlete Chorila at the ninth Amsterdam Games in 1928. However, they failed to break Darley's world record of 4 minutes 47 seconds. Nevertheless, Gulub's strength was evident here. Darley also displayed the prestige of a world record holder, and both were worthy of being called famous athletes.

Interest Remains in Swimming 109

(Dentsu, Los Angeles, 11th) With only three days remaining in the Olympic Games, the focus of interest has been captured by aquatic sports. The overcrowded stands of the past few days have dwindled to three or four thousand people, mostly those with a particular interest in lacrosse and other sports. Therefore, those who maintain the vibrant atmosphere of the grand sports arena since the opening of the games are the participating athletes, sports officials, and journalists. There is still the lacrosse final in track and field, but there is no doubt that India will dominate, as they excel in this sport and have no equal. They will surely bring glory to all of East Asia. In addition, fencing is becoming increasingly exciting, with French, Italian, and German fencers taking the lead. In rowing at Los Angeles Bay and equestrian at Rivarne, Europe had a monopoly until the previous Olympics. This year, Japan and the United States have sent excellent horses to participate, and the outcome is uncertain. The most interesting event of the day will be the men's 1500-meter freestyle preliminary. In the quest for the "King of the Water," the participating Japanese athletes, such as Makino, Kitamura, and Ishizu, claim they will exhibit their best long-distance swimming to avenge the shame of the 400-meter event. The Argentine athlete, to protect his world record created by General Rila from being surpassed, has abandoned the 400-meter event to concentrate all his efforts on the 1500-meter event. When experts encounter each other, a spectacular sight is sure to unfold. The French "Dragon King" Jianli, as well as the first-place finisher of the previous Olympics, Gulub, who set a new world record in the 400-meter event, and Australian Charlton are also not easy opponents. In the 200-meter breaststroke, Japan is the record-holding country and has the best chance of winning. Tsuruta, Koike, and Nakagawa have vowed to participate with the intention of winning, full of spirit. However, Finland's Rhinefall, in addition to Spans, are also formidable opponents. The men's 100-meter backstroke will hold its semi-finals today. With Kiyokawa's record from yesterday, there is also great hope. However, the American Kabasa, etc., are also veterans in this field. The competition for the championship will surely be between the Japanese and American teams.

Local News

Ministry of Education Commends the City Education Bureau 114

For Handling Refugee Education (Central News Agency) After the January 28th Incident, refugees from the war zone were rescued by various groups in the city and settled in Shanghai, reaching over 100,000 people at one point, with tens of thousands remaining for long-term care. The City Education Bureau, recognizing that out-of-school children and illiterate adults accounted for more than half of the entire refugee population, seized the opportunity to provide appropriate education and instill the meaning of resisting the enemy and saving the country. It also compiled 22 lessons of teaching materials, each with illustrations and meanings that were highly alert. The Ministry of Education considered that the bureau had taken advantage of the opportunity during the Japanese invasion of Shanghai to implement short-term public education, which was commendable, and issued a special commendation yesterday.

The junior high school of the Shanghai Fudan Experimental Middle School relocated to Hangzhou last semester due to the impact of the war. It has now returned to its original location within Fudan University in Jiangwan. The school buildings have been repaired and restored to their original condition. They are now actively working on replenishing the library, laboratories, and specimen rooms. In addition, students who were unable to attend the school last semester due to the distance have been requesting to return, and quite a few have registered. Therefore, a spring semester class has been added for the first and second years of the senior high general course and the first year of the business course. As the junior high school students are younger and commuting is inconvenient, the school has established a junior high school campus at 55 Kang Nao Road (west end of Gordon Road) in the Public Concession. The library, playground, specimen room, dormitories, and classrooms have been fully arranged, and many students from near and far have enthusiastically registered.

Records of the Ancient Temple Bell: Bu Chu Ting Cao Zhai Fu (72) 118

79 When Mr. Zhu and Dr. Tang met, there were inevitably some pleasantries, which I have omitted, focusing only on their discussions of questions and difficulties. Dr. Tang first asked Mr. Zhu about my words: (Since your village advocates production, it seems appropriate to use new machines and learn from foreign countries head-on in order to generate great effects. Why do you still use handicrafts?) Mr. Zhu said: (Learning from foreign countries head-on means thoroughly learning the entire process, which is the right way. For example, using Western methods to print books requires learning everything from afforestation to papermaking, to steelmaking, to making printing presses and using large machines to print. If you only learn machine printing, then you will not have steel to make machines, or wood to make paper. As a result, running a printing house or newspaper office will require buying foreign machines and foreign paper. Therefore, printing houses and newspaper offices become large-scale sales organizations for foreign paper, and even their own lives are controlled by foreign paper merchants. Learning from foreign countries head-on means first learning how to afforest, make paper, make steel, and make machines, and then learning how to use large machines for printing. Before learning how to make paper, make steel, and make machines, jumping directly to learning how to use large machines for printing is extremely dangerous. So, in my opinion, there is an order to learning from foreign countries head-on, and if this order is reversed, instability in the industrial world will occur. One of the production activities advocated in our village is everything from planting cotton to tailoring. The planting of cotton adopts the latest scientific methods, while spinning, weaving, and tailoring are still done by hand. However, in handicrafts, we also strive to improve technology.) Dr. Tang said: (How can cloth woven by hand compete with products made by machines?) Mr. Zhu said: (How does the competition between automobiles and sedan chairs fare?) Dr. Tang said: (Of course, automobiles win and sedan chairs lose. Shanghai has not had a single sedan chair since 1929.) Mr. Zhu said: (Shanghai does not have a single sedan chair, but it has many handcarts. Automobiles can drive away sedan chairs, but they cannot drive away handcarts. What is the reason for this? People who used to ride in sedan chairs have switched to riding in automobiles, so automobiles are suitable for survival, and sedan chairs are naturally eliminated. People who ride in handcarts can still only afford to ride in handcarts and cannot afford to ride in automobiles, so handcarts are still suitable for survival, and although automobiles are fierce, they cannot defeat handcarts. Machines can only defeat some handicrafts, and some are not easily defeated. Is that right?)

Manchu Proverbs and Prophecies 119

— Zhan Lu

The short fellow of jokes and anecdotes has put forward a puppet-like Manchu state. People in society feel that the commonly used Manchu proverbs are very mysterious and want to explore the door to this mystery. According to their views, there are the following interpretations: "Sweating profusely." | This sentence should be applied to Puyi. His going to be the puppet head of Manchuria is "sweating profusely." "Da Khan" means great Khan, which means that he has not awakened from his imperial dream. "Manchu rice is good to eat, Manchu language is difficult to speak." | The short fellow forcefully points out that the people outside the customs are Manchus, which is extremely ridiculous. Manchus have already assimilated with the Chinese. Most of the people in the Northeast are from Hebei and Shandong. They live in Manchuria, but they can only eat Manchu rice and cannot speak the Manchu language. It really calls for "Manchu rice is good to eat, Manchu language is difficult to speak." "One wrong move leads to a complete loss." | These two sentences should of course be applied to the non-resistant Northeast authorities: one wrong move has led to the loss of the entire Manchurian territory. "A full load of sesame seeds is spilled, scraping from the sugar cake." | These two sentences should also be applied to the Northeast authorities: he lost all of Manchuria, which is like spilling a full load of sesame seeds; but he wants to scrape sesame seeds from the sugar cake to compensate for his losses. One telegram in the morning asks for tens of thousands, and one telegram in the evening asks for tens of thousands. These are like sesame seeds on the sugar cake, and even if they are scraped clean, they cannot make up for the spilled full load of sesame seeds. If you want sesame seeds, you should go out of the customs and take a trip.

Yang the Beggar's Road Building Story 120

— Zizai

Yang San. A native of northern Sichuan. Ten years ago, due to difficult living conditions, he became a beggar. He wandered to Yongxing Court in southern Sichuan, begging from door to door, sleeping in the open air, and spending his life as a beggar. He felt that the roads were rugged and narrow, which caused many inconveniences for merchants and travelers. So, he carried a hoe and shovel to make them flat. Over time, he became familiar with the local people and the land, and various circles in the local area helped him slightly. Yang took the opportunity to solicit donations and hire workers to repair the roads. With twenty yuan, he repaired a section of road worth twenty yuan. With ten yuan, he repaired a section of road worth ten yuan. Whether it was sunny or rainy, he supervised the work by the side of the road and also participated in the operation. In tattered clothes and worn-out shoes, his hands and feet were calloused. He never took any money from the donations for his own food and clothing, and he still went out to beg for food. He was clear about public and private matters and never took a penny dishonestly. Therefore, people far and near respected him. When they heard that he was coming, they often helped him generously. Even young children and old people with white hair called him Yang the Benevolent. His transformative power was such that for several years, rich merchants and gentry from Zigong knew that he was honest and impartial, did good deeds widely, and benefited travelers. They all donated money to help. Whenever Yang went to someone's house, he had a smiling face. Before he could open his mouth, they were often generous and happy to help without hesitation. In the past ten years, he has built more than three hundred li of trunk roads. The number of branch roads is countless, from Xufu Diao Huanglou, Zongchang Datieya, Yongxingchang Baihuachang Wubao Town to Zigong Liangjing and other places. They have all become flat and prosperous. Travelers say it is convenient. The road from Zigong to Yibin was originally paved with stone slabs. Thirty years ago, it was repaired by Li Heng. Over time, it became dilapidated. Fortunately, Yang the Benevolent raised funds to repair it, and the road became flat. Yang became ill due to overwork and lay in bed at Guan Yu Temple in Yongxingchang. He died of illness. He Runmin, the head of Baihua Town, felt sorry for his tragic experience and admired his behavior. In addition to donating clothes and coffins, he also launched a memorial service for him. Alas. Building bridges and repairing roads accumulates blessings in heaven. Although Yang the Benevolent was a beggar, he was able to benefit others as his responsibility. Although his physical body has died, his name will be forever known. This is a record of it.

Even those who tried to imitate her secretly could not match her. Therefore, after the Double Ninth Festival, her door was filled with customers every day. If one was late, the chicken was sold out. One had to order the night before to get it. Such was the prosperity of her business, and one can imagine how skillful her cooking was. Every year when winter came, Liaogong almost never missed a day to call his friends to Li's tavern, killing a chicken to enjoy with drinks.
