On Lotus Root 123

— Xu Wanhua

Among the red flower lotus roots, it is a cool and refreshing world to escape the summer heat, and the beautiful woman's snow-white lotus root is especially a wonderful product to wash away the heat and soothe the spleen. In the past, when I was a guest in Green Willow City, to pass the hot summer, I would always punt a boat on the slender West Lake. Choosing a deep place in the lotus shade, I placed myself in the midst of ten thousand greens. At times, a refreshing breeze would greet me, and a delicate fragrance would enter my sleeves. Opening my shirt to the wind, it was a different world. I would then buy freshly picked tender lotus roots from the misty waves, slice them, and eat them. The coolness would penetrate my teeth and cheeks, enough to relieve the thirst of the literary garden. Looking at the scenery and feeling emotions, I would vaguely see a lotus arm half-bent, from last night's sweet pillow. Chewing on this, there was even more aftertaste.

The relationship between lotus root and emotional people has been widely praised by poets. This is because it emerges from the filthy mud without being stained, maintaining its sacred purity. It is just like emotional people using noble love and pure integrity to break through dark and difficult environments and stand in the same position. To the exquisite heart, it is good at spitting out affectionate silk. Even if the body is divided, the silk is still connected. As for emotional people, ("spring silkworm until death the silk ceases,") ("the heart has a spiritual rhinoceros a little penetrates"). They also have the same sympathy for each other. This is why lotus root is valued by emotional people and prepared as the only food during intimate moments.

Lotus root is of great benefit to health. Those sold in cities, either because they have been out of the water for a long time or because of climate changes, it seems more difficult to find those with complete color, fragrance, and taste. Those who eat it should store it in a hanging container and immerse it in a deep well, which can preserve much of the original flavor. Lotus roots in the shape of linked branches are wonderful gifts for lovers, no less than a knot of unity and a jade ring. However, they are not easy to obtain. There are also descendants lotus roots, with small branches clustered on the giant stalk, like arhats. Lovers often offer them on the banquet table during the Qixi Festival to worship the Cowherd and Weaver Girl and during the Mid-Autumn Festival to worship the moon, in order to pray for children and blessings.

West Lake lotus root, along with the lake scenery, has been praised. Its lotus root powder, when eaten, is mixed with rock sugar and boiling water. At noon, it is used instead of tea, which can clear the lungs and intestines, aid digestion, and dispel heat and remove烦恼. It is truly a supreme drink. Or, glutinous rice is stuffed into the lotus root holes, cooked, sliced, and sprinkled with sugar. In addition, the soup left over from cooking the lotus root is used to cook fragrant rice into porridge. Sipping lotus root porridge with lotus root dishes is fragrant, sweet, and palatable, penetrating the heart and spleen. This is also a new innovation, which can supplement what the food book does not cover.

Random Talk on Goldfish 124

— Wu Jiren

Not being able to wake up early in the morning is also very related to the body. Therefore, I use raising goldfish to remind myself. I know that in everyone's mind, it often happens like this. When you admire something, you will be entangled and worried about it all the time. Therefore, my morning goldfish watching has become a daily routine.

I remember one morning, when I was leaning over to look at the small fish in the tank, I felt that the small fish had a particularly large appetite. I gave them a lot of red worms, and they were all eaten up in less than a quarter of an hour. The development of small fish is also divided into fast and slow. Those hatched in the same period differ greatly in size in less than a week. A few of the larger ones couldn't find food to eat, and their little bellies were not full. Therefore, they would even indiscriminately harm the smaller ones of their kind. The smaller ones couldn't swim fast and couldn't avoid it, so they had to let it be slaughtered, let it be swallowed whole. The innocent little fish had their tails and eyes eaten up. Looking at them, only some游气 was left. Those few fierce ones still didn't let them live. They went further and further, eating their intestines, heart, liver, and bone fragments, leaving nothing behind. Only then did they triumphantly go to chase other fish. I couldn't stand it, so I caught those few strong and domineering ones and separated them, so there was no tragedy of fish cannibalizing each other.

Later, when I thought about it, fish are ignorant and unconscious aquatic animals, yet their nature allows them to kill each other. No wonder humans do the same. Originally, no matter if it's a group, an assembly, a town, or even a province, a country, or the whole world, what justice is there to talk about? Isn't it the same as fish, where the strong bully the weak? Fish do it because they have no food to eat. As for people, the scope is too broad. But when you think about it carefully, it's all for the problem of food, clothing, and shelter. It's a pity that there aren't people like the goldfish watcher to mediate for them one by one.

Records of Things Seen and Heard in the Old Capital 125

— Zhu An

Seal Paste Recently, there is a Wu Disheng who claims to have obtained the method of making seal paste from Mr. Li of the Imperial Household Department of the Forbidden City. Using the secrets not passed down within the inner court, he makes seal paste and sells it at a very high price. He also wrote a book detailing the method. Introduced by a friend, I spent ten yuan to get one tael, which was still cheap. His products are deep red and vibrant, the same in winter and summer, which is truly his specialty. According to his description, selecting materials is the priority in making paste, and choosing oil is the most urgent. The oil must be aged, and it must be naturally aged, not artificially. He claims to have obtained a bottle of oil from a certain residence, which was yellow, a thing from the Qianlong period, with the number and weight of the Imperial Household Department. With this precious oil, he used moxa floss and willow catkins as the base, used high-quality cinnabar as the color, and added gems and gold leaf to assist it. After it is made, it must be buried three feet deep in the soil for half a year before being used. He also said that he planned to continue making seal paste with red gold, coral, male essence, lapis lazuli, turquoise, malachite, and crystal. He expects himself to be a revolution in seal paste. There are many eccentric people in the old capital. Even the slightest interest has those who study it all their lives. I record this to broaden the strange news.

Fayuan Temple 126

Many temples in the northern capital possess good fields and beautiful products. They have good connections and live in wealth. They are proud of this. This is all a habit formed by emperors, eunuchs, nobles, and relatives who flatter the Buddha. When there is a lot of property, there is always competition. The pure realm is turned into a den of fame and fortune. In recent years, the Fayuan Temple in the south of the city is the one with temple property that has triggered disputes. The temple was where Emperor Taizong of Tang Dynasty prayed for the soldiers who conquered the East, so it is called Minzhong. Xie Fangde was also imprisoned in this temple when he was arrested and brought to Yan. It is truly the oldest stupa in Beijing. The inscriptions on the tablets of other temples cannot surpass the Yuan Dynasty. However, this place alone has a Tang Dynasty tablet. Moreover, the courtyards are quiet and peaceful, the flowers and trees are lush, and famous people have left inscriptions, calligraphy, paintings, and literary playthings, which are the best in the capital. Literary men and poets have always enjoyed praising it. Today, the temple is still famous for its lilacs. When they bloom, the purple color is like a steaming glow, and the fragrance touches the sleeves. The essence of blue is the best, and it is finally called the head. However, the prosperity of a hundred years ago is not comparable to today. The Beijing Miscellaneous Records says. (On the eighth day of the fourth month of the year, the Minzhong Temple in the southern city holds a life release conference. Wealthy merchants, women, and wives of prominent officials wear elaborate makeup and beautiful clothes, and gather like bees. Frivolous teenagers act like they are visiting a brothel. Cars hit the grain and people rub shoulders. The monks guarding the door ask for 200 coins from those who enter, otherwise they are refused. Thus, green and red are marked, and shoes are intertwined. Pearls are lost and emeralds fall, and powder and grease flow. The monasteries seem like the Zhen and Wei rivers. The monks also give each child brought by the women a piggy bank, enticing them to bring it back full and send it to the meeting next year. Thus, the gold earned in one day amounts to thousands. Those who say that it is a life release conference only buy a few sparrows and release them. In reality, there is nothing to see. Later, a certain censor presented a memorial to ban it, and it was abolished.) In recent years, the prosperity of Buddhist affairs is not in Fayuan, but in Guangji. This is also an old temple from the Jin Dynasty. It has been in disrepair for a long time. In the early years of the Republic of China, the powerful people in power raised money to rebuild it, and it became a garden of gold. Guests with swords and shoes, and the faces of powder and dai, come together in droves. The secular dust is tangible. The bad habits of hundreds of years still remain in this tail sound. I am afraid that it will not be long before it will be like the Fayuan Temple, only for passers-by to mourn.

The Terrifying Fall in Finance and Gold Market 127

A Wild Drop of Fifteen Taels and Four Mace

Total Drop of Over Thirty-Three Taels in Three Days The gold standard capital drop is intensifying, infinitely changing, with shocking waves that cannot be suppressed. At every turn, the price swings three or four taels high or low. The entire day has ten taels of price swings. Industry intentions are confused and payment is unstable, leading to an extremely chaotic market situation. The final wild drop was greater than fifteen taels. Silver prices, contrary to yesterday's expectation of reduction, rose. This was especially due to the frequent buying in the US for forward silver. This caused the gold price to immediately drop by more than ten taels, breaking through 720 taels. The selling wind in the market grew even stronger, almost due to the extreme looseness of foreign exchange. However, short sellers seized this opportunity to make some gains. The exchange rates of the UK and US both seem to have recovered. Even though fellow traders were selling heavily, bank appetite remained unceasing. This led to a recovery of more than seven taels. At noon, the softening reappeared. The later market went from stable to weak, truly due to the selling party exceeding the Heng standard. Further, exchange rates were especially loose. Panic reigned in the market, causing a sudden drop of six or seven taels. It finally broke 710 taels. In the end, there was a slight recovery of three to five taels, hovering around twelve or thirteen taels. The tumbling trend has no certainty. The details of the entire day are recorded below.

Open at wild drop of twelve taels and seven mace The market opened in the morning for September contracts with a wild drop of twelve taels and seven mace, to 715 and a half taels. About a quarter of an hour later, Zeng Zhongming, Deputy Minister of Railways, also arrived. However, Wang himself was not at home, so in addition to the above-mentioned people, Chen Bijun, Wang's wife, represented Wang in the discussion. They talked for about an hour before they all left and returned to their residences. As for the content of the discussion, see Zhou Gengsheng's statement for details.

Zhou Gengsheng's Talk Zhou Gengsheng, the representative of Chiang Kai-shek, arrived in Shanghai yesterday. He once went to visit Wang with Ju Zheng, He Yingqin, and others, and brought Chiang's handwritten letter to Wang, but he did not get to meet him. A reporter from the New Voice Society specifically visited Zhou's residence yesterday afternoon. According to the talk, he came to Shanghai to handle the affairs of Wuhan University. He met Chiang Kai-shek when he left Wuhan. Chiang's expression on Wang's resignation was very clear, that is, he hoped that Wang would quickly resume his position. When he met Wang's wife, Ms. Chen Bijun, today (i.e., yesterday), there were no results. What he talked about was only the personal talks of the representatives and ministers. However, Wang's resignation may not be effective with empty words of retention, and a practical solution must be found to be appropriate.

Zeng Zhongming's Talk Zeng Zhongming made the following statement to reporters yesterday: (1) Mr. Wang has left Shanghai to go to the countryside to recuperate, expressing his extremely firm attitude. Wang has no intention of resuming his position as President of the Executive Yuan at this time, and extremely hopes that Zhang Xueliang will resign and quickly select a successor to the new President of the Executive Yuan to avoid the long-term suspension of the central government. (2) The central government is unanimously advocating Zhang's resignation in terms of public opinion. For example, the Central Daily News, the New Kyoto Daily News, etc., have very clear expressions. However, in the Shanghai press, there seems to be a general idea that they want to speak but dare not. The central government is now the same as the Shanghai opinion faction on this point, because this point also has its unspeakable pain. (3) After Zhang's resignation, the Military Affairs Commission has not heard of any acceptance. If the central government officially approves Zhang's resignation, Wang will no longer be the President of the Executive Yuan, because this is the trial implementation of democracy. (4) Whether the ministers who sympathize with Mr. Wang will advance and retreat with Wang in the future is still uncertain at this time. It depends on the situation in the future. (5) I learned about Tang Youren's visit to Wuhan in the newspaper, and I heard that Wang's letter to Chiang was brought there. (6) I will briefly observe in Shanghai this time and will return to Nanjing tonight (i.e., last night).

Song Ziwen's Actions Song Ziwen, Minister of Finance, left for Hongqiao Airport at 6:30 yesterday morning, accompanied by Shen Dexie, Director of the Aircraft Factory, Mao Bangchu, President of the Aviation School, and five Westerners, driven by Mao Bangchu. The privately-owned Sikorsky plane departed, advanced along the Shanghai-Hangzhou line, and did not return to Shanghai until about 10 am at noon. It is reported that Song went to Hangzhou to inspect the newly built airport in Hangzhou. However, according to another rumor, Song went to Hangzhou to meet Wang Jingwei, or pre-arranged a meeting with Chairman Chiang, but because it was not confirmed, he did not dare to make a definite decision. However, Song's assistants are very secretive, and it seems that the latter statement may not be without reason.

Tang Youren Returns to Shanghai Tang Youren, Secretary-General of the Central Political Conference, flew to Wuhan the day before yesterday to meet with Chiang Kai-shek, Chairman of the Military Affairs Commission, and represented Wang in all matters. At 2:30 pm yesterday, Tang still took a China Airlines plane from Wuhan to Shanghai. Those who came with him included Huang Renlin, Director-General of the Nanjing Lizhi Society, and others. After Tang got off the plane, he took a Shanghai car from Longhua Airport and went straight to the Huaan Hotel to rest. Then he went to Wang's secret residence to visit Wang and reported on the progress of the talks. Tang did not return to his private residence in Yuyangli until late at night.

Newspaper Erroneously Reported the Escape of the Resident Police in Baziqiao 148

The Municipal Government Protests Yesterday 149

Regarding the News of (The Increasingly Deteriorating Feelings of Chinese People Towards Japan) The Central News Agency also requested that each newspaper be careful in publishing it in the future. Since the Japanese newspapers in this port published the news of the escape of the patrol police from the Baziqiao Public Security Bureau branch, other rumors have arisen, and the hearts of the people in Zhabei have been floating again. The municipal government believes that this matter is completely unfounded and should be seriously corrected to stabilize people's hearts. At 4 pm the day before yesterday (10th), he specially protested to Murai Kuramatsu, the Japanese Consul-General in Shanghai. The copy of the protest letter is as follows: I would like to inform you that on the 6th of this month, the Japanese newspapers Shanghai Daily News, Shanghai Mainichi News, and Shanghai Daily News all published a news item about the escape of the patrol police from the Baziqiao Public Security Bureau branch. After investigating, the matters stated are all untrue facts, which are obviously shaking the hearts of the people in this city. If this is not corrected, the impact will be worrying. It is appropriate to write to your Consul-General and strictly order each newspaper to correct the records and order them to pay attention in the future. On the same day, the Shanghai Mainichi News and the Shanghai Daily News published a news item (The Increasingly Deteriorating Feelings of Chinese People Towards Japan), writing about a few trivial disputes between Chinese and Japanese people to conclude that the feelings of Chinese and Japanese people are deteriorating. Now, regardless of whether the content is true or not, this kind of record is enough to increase the ill will between the people of China and Japan, and I believe that your Consul-General also knows this deeply. It is also hoped that your Consul-General will forward this to each newspaper and ask them to be careful in publishing this kind of news in order to promote friendship. It is appropriate to enclose the records of the above-mentioned newspapers and send them to you. I hope that you will investigate and handle them and reply. This is addressed to Murai Kuramatsu, Japanese Consul-General in Shanghai, with the seal of Wu Tiecheng, Mayor of Shanghai.

Verdict on the Yun Huifang Case 151

Sentenced to Two Months Imprisonment, Suspended for Two Years

The First Special Court Brought Yun Back Yesterday

｜Also Accused in the Bomb Plot Against Yu Ruiliang｜Yun Huifang, a member of the "Blood Soul Assassination Squad" and a teenager from Changzhou, learned that the Maochang Foreign Goods Store, opened by Ningbo native Shen Maochun at 347 Fahua Republic Road in the French Concession, was secretly selling Japanese goods. On the evening of the 5th of this month at 9 p.m., she took a hand grenade and threw it at the store, damaging the glass and floor. Yun was intercepted by the Chinese police on patrol and detained at the Second Precinct, Second District, of the Public Security Bureau in Chenxiangge. The French Concession Police Department's Political Section sent Chinese and Western detectives to bring Yun back to the police station. They also went with Chinese and Western detectives from the Xinzha Police Station of the Public Concession to Yun's residence at 207 Heng'an Lane, Qingdao Road, Parker Road, where they seized another bomb similar to the one used in the bombing, and deposited it at the Xinzha Police Station. The French Concession Police then sent Yun to the Second Special District Court, and prosecuted her for the crimes of endangering peace, forming a secret society, and causing damage, under Articles 158, 161, and 382 of the Criminal Code. The presiding judge of the Criminal Court, Wang Gangxu, together with Prosecutor Wu Xiaoke, held a court hearing. The defendant, Yun Huifang, was defended by three lawyers: Zhao Chen, Shen Junru, and Liu Hongxun. The Municipal Chamber of Commerce also sent a letter and a representative to the court, requesting leniency for the defendant. The debate was declared closed and a date was set for sentencing. The defendant was ordered to provide two shopkeepers as guarantors, which has already been reported. Yesterday was the date of sentencing. The defendant and her lawyers arrived at the court at 9 a.m. to await the verdict. At 10 a.m., Judge Wang, accompanied by Court Clerk Fang, came to Criminal Court One and called the defendant to the stand. After briefly questioning her age, origin, occupation, and address, he announced the verdict. The main text stated: "Yun Huifang is sentenced to two months of imprisonment, suspended for two years, for the two crimes of threatening others with harm to their lives and property, causing danger." After the sentencing, Luo Bo (transliteration), Deputy Western Inspector of the General Inspectorate of the Public Concession Police Department, along with Deputy Chinese Inspector Liu Shaokui, and Deputy Inspectors Wang Debiao and Zhao Bingkun, and bailiffs from the First Special Court, claimed that the defendant was also involved in the case of plotting to bomb Yu Ruiliang at 729-731 Xinzha Road in the Public Concession at 7:30 a.m. on July 28. They requested that she be transferred to their custody for investigation and presented a letter from Zhou Xianjue, President of the First Special Court. Judge Wang examined the letter and ordered the defendant to be temporarily detained. The letter would be sent to the President of the Court for consideration. The lawyers immediately objected, but to no avail. At around 1 p.m., she was transferred to the Fuzhou Road General Inspectorate of the Public Concession. Lawyers Zhao Chen and Shen Junru, and Jiang Junyi, a representative from Changzhou, visited the Chinese and Western inspectors one after another to negotiate for her release, but were unsuccessful. Yun was still being treated well inside. It is said that she will be sent to the First District Local Court for trial at 9 a.m. today. Lawyer Li Zuyu will join the legal team. The official letter from the First Special District, signed by Zhou Xianjue, President of the First Special Court, stated that according to the General Inspectorate of the Public Works Department, the defendant Yun Huifang plotted to harm Yu Ruiliang with a bomb at 729-731 Xinzha Road at 7:30 a.m. on July 28. She is currently detained in the Second Special District Local Court, and they requested her transfer. Accordingly, they dispatched a detective with a letter to request clarification and to have Yun Huifang handed over to the detective to be brought back for handling.

The Slowdown Strike at the China Merchants Inland River Machinery Factory is Resolved 153

Due to unpaid wages, the factory workers at the China Merchants Bureau's Inland River Machinery Factory demanded cash payment, leading to a slowdown strike by all workers. Yesterday, General Manager Li Guojie ordered the accounting department to raise some cash, and at the same time set a date for full payment. He also persuaded the workers to return to work first to avoid hindering operations. The workers resumed work at 3 p.m. The situation is described in detail below:

Main Reason for the Slowdown Strike: The China Merchants Inland River Machinery Factory is located in Lujiazui, Pudong. Repairs to the Bureau's inland river vessels and minor work on major ocean-going vessels have always been handled by the factory's workers. The factory also undertakes repairs for commercial vessels outside the Bureau. Since Li Guojie took office as General Manager, he has been very considerate of the lower-level workers, paying wages monthly, which the workers were quite satisfied with. However, the accounting department issued a check for 8,000 yuan for the June wages, but it was not cashed due to a shortage of cash. The workers repeatedly requested payment, but it was not paid. By the afternoon of the 10th, the workers began a slowdown strike.

Demand for Cash Payment: On the afternoon of the 10th, all the workers at the Inland River Machinery Factory went on a slowdown strike. All work in the factory was completely stopped. The ships waiting for repair in the dock were also stopped. The workers elected representatives to demand payment from the new Factory Manager Xing Qixin, stating that the workers' wages were limited, and they relied entirely on their meager wages. If payment was delayed, their lives would be difficult. They requested cash payment, and the slowdown strike was not their intention. Factory Manager Xing reported this to the General Manager.

Allocation of Funds: Yesterday morning, Xing Qixin went to the General Bureau and reported to Li Guojie on the factory workers' slowdown strike and their request for wages. General Manager Li stated that since he took office, he had never delayed the monthly wages of the workers. The accounting department's issuance of checks this time was to regulate finances, and cash payments would be made in a few days. He immediately ordered the accounting department to allocate 2,000 yuan in cash to be distributed to the workers by the Factory Manager. The remaining amount would be paid in full on the 15th.

Resumption of Work in the Afternoon: Work at the machinery factory is related to shipping. Xing Qixin gathered the workers and the representatives conveyed General Manager Li's intentions, that a portion of the wages would be paid first, and the remainder would be paid in full on the 15th of this month. The workers were satisfied. After receiving their wages yesterday, they all resumed work at 3 p.m. A slowdown strike came to an end, or so it seems.

British Public Bus Workers Went on Strike Yesterday Morning 154

Because the Company Did Not Fulfill Its Promise of a Wage Increase

A Strike Committee Was Formed and a Strike Declaration Was Issued

The Company Dismissed All Striking Workers. All ticket collectors of the British-owned Chinese Public Bus Company in the Public Concession went on strike yesterday morning, opposing the company's failure to fulfill its promise to increase wages and demanding the reinstatement of dismissed workers. They formed a strike committee and issued a declaration, presenting their conditions. The company held an emergency board meeting and reluctantly maintained traffic with a notice, dismissing all striking workers. The situation is very serious. The details are recorded below:

Background: All the ticket collectors opposed the company's oppression and went on strike last year. However, due to the harsh environment, they announced an unconditional return to work. In June of this year, the company's factory manager and transportation manager, Xiao Date, directly negotiated with the workers' representatives. If the workers did not skim money, the company would increase wages. At that time, the workers' representatives stated that they would not skim money after the wage increase. Starting from the 8th of this month, the company changed the 1, 9, and 10 bus routes to segment fares and issued a notice to the workers, saying, "(Because the practice of ticket collectors' embezzlement is becoming more and more serious, the factory manager and others have repeatedly advised the representatives. Before the ticket collectors can change their ways and stop embezzling, there is no possibility of raising wages. After the Sino-Japanese War, business has plummeted. Our company still protects all employees without layoffs, which is comforting to the staff. Therefore, if the ticket collectors can improve themselves and never embezzle, to assist the company, the company will seriously consider rewarding them. This is to inform all ticket collectors, take note, Factory Manager Xiao Date)."

Conditions Presented: The ticket collectors were very angry about the company's notice, believing that the company did not fulfill its promise to increase wages. They specially invited representatives from steelworkers, drivers, and ticket inspectors to the Jiuyunxuan Restaurant the day before yesterday to discuss unified action and propose requirements. The requirements were jointly proposed by the representatives of each department, and each department unanimously demanded the signing of a strike agreement, expressing sympathy for the ticket collector strike. The conditions are recorded below: (A) Ticket Selling Conditions: (1) No worker shall be dismissed. All workers dismissed by Bill shall be reinstated immediately. (2) Increase wages to 40 yuan, with an annual increase of 3 yuan. (3) Restore the copper coin bonus, issued according to the original standard. Wages shall be paid during the strike period. (4) All new cards shall be exchanged, and shall be exchanged every six months thereafter. (B) Ticket Inspection Conditions: (1) Increase wages to a minimum of 50 yuan. (2) Working hours shall not exceed eight hours. (3) Restore the work of ticket inspector No. 66 and dismiss Bill. (4) Suspension with a one-year severance pay.

Strike Committee Formed: The ticket collectors held a joint meeting the night before last, organizing a strike committee, including a presidium, secretariat, propaganda department, disciplinary department, communication department, transportation department, and a fund management committee. The heads of each department, as well as the chairman and fund committee members, were immediately elected. A strike order was issued, and the collection of strike funds began. Each ticket collector paid one yuan to the fund. It was decided that the official strike would begin at 5:00 a.m. on the 11th. All disciplinary departments would be deployed to establish the strike committee's office and branch offices for each department's representatives.

Strike Order: After the strike committee announced the strike on the 11th the night before last, the transportation team separately notified the workers, and an emergency meeting was held at Jinshuilou. It was decided to send four representatives to the General Company on the Bund to present the conditions. At the same time, all the masses were mobilized to participate. The disciplinary team prepared to use force to expel the White Russians who were undermining the strike, earnestly uniting all the workers, including coppersmiths and drivers, to take unified action. An excerpt from the strike declaration is recorded below: The fact that imperialism is intensifying its oppression of workers after the war points out that increasing fares intensifies the exploitation of Chinese passengers, launching a unified attack on workers and passengers. It reiterates that the White Russians are destroying the interests of the workers and are lackeys of capital. Finally, it declares that this strike is to fight for conditions for the workers themselves and to win glory for the Republic of China. It earnestly requests all sectors and all Shanghai workers to provide practical assistance.

Buses Stop Running: At 5:00 a.m. yesterday, all the ticket collectors, and Korean ticket inspectors, carried out the strike order of the strike committee, and all routes of the public buses, including Route 1 from Jing'an Temple to Bazizhang, Route 2 from Eryangjing Bridge to Bazizilu, Route 3 from Caojiadu to Nanyang University, Route 4 from Jing'an Temple to Hongqiao, Route 5 from North Railway Station to Sanmaoge Bridge, Route 6 from Tilanqiao to Bazizhang, Route 7 from Caojiadu to Beixinjing, Route 9 from Jing'an Temple to the Electric Light Factory, Route 10 from Caojiadu to Yinxiangxiang, and ABCDE Special Express, A1 Special Bus, Jing'an Temple to Waibaidu Bridge, had to be completely stopped due to the lack of ticket sellers.

Board Meeting: The British-owned Chinese Public Bus Company held an emergency board meeting at 10:00 a.m. yesterday. First, Factory Manager Xiao Date reported on the workers' strike. It was decided on the spot: (1) To notify the striking workers that those who were absent from work on the 11th would be dismissed. (2) To find ways to restore the operation of all bus routes to facilitate traffic.

Notice to All Sectors: The British Public Bus Company issued a notice yesterday, saying, "Since our company changed to segmented fares, the ticket sellers took advantage of the opportunity to embezzle, and this morning (August 11) all abandoned their posts and went on an unconditional strike, resulting in our company being able to run only a very small number of vehicles, causing great inconvenience to the public. We feel deeply ashamed. In the shortest possible time and within the possible scope, our company will do its best to restore traffic to its original state, in order to live up to the expectations of all sectors."

Overall Dismissal: The British Public Bus Company announced yesterday that ticket sellers who were absent from work on August 11 would be dismissed. They should submit their uniforms and miscellaneous items. This announcement was made by Factory Manager and Transportation Manager Xiao Date.

Pledge Not to Resume Work: A reporter from Xinsheng News Agency met with members of the strike committee yesterday. According to the released statement, the life of workers such as bus ticket sellers, drivers, ticket inspectors, sweepers, and coppersmiths is extremely miserable, with an average monthly salary of less than 20 yuan. Since the Shanghai Incident, the company has dismissed a large number of workers. In the past nine months, almost all the old ticket sellers have been replaced. The company also dismissed two drivers and one ticket inspector, and implemented changes in ticket colors, increased fares, and increased the work of workers, to

Page 14

the point that the workers could not bear it any longer, and proposed conditions. The company had no sincerity in accepting, and instead prepared to dismiss everyone. Therefore, they had no choice but to announce a strike to awaken the company. Now the company has announced the dismissal of the strikers, but the strikers are determined to fight to the death and will not resume work until their goals are achieved.

Reluctant Traffic: From 1:00 p.m. yesterday, in order to maintain traffic and facilitate transportation, the company assigned ticket inspectors and checkers to perform ticket selling work, reluctantly running 14 buses on Route 1, 6 on A1, 5 on Route 2, 4 on Route 5, 20 on Route 9, 2 on A, 1 on C, 2 on B, and 1 on D. The rest were still suspended. They returned to the factory early at 8:00 p.m. As for the company's entrance on Kangnuo Road, police officers from the Sixth District of the Municipal Public Security Bureau and detectives from the Gordon Road Police Station were stationed there to provide protection.

Conflict Between Workers of the Sanyou Industrial Society on Nanjing Road and Detectives 155

Three Arrested Were Released Immediately

Petitioned the Municipal Government in the Afternoon

The Social Affairs Bureau Convened Interrogation. After the Yinxiangxiang Sanyou Industrial Factory announced its closure, all the workers demanded the resumption of work, resulting in disputes. Although the Party and government organs repeatedly mediated, it has not been resolved yet. Because the company reduced the workers' food expenses, the workers went to the Nanjing Road retail department to petition yesterday morning, resulting in a conflict with the Western police, and seven people were injured. At that time, the situation was serious, and traffic was interrupted. In the afternoon, all the workers went to the Municipal Government to petition, and dispersed in the evening.

Reduced Food Expenses: After the Shanghai factory of the Sanyou Industrial Society was closed, the Municipal Government ordered the company to maintain food expenses. The Social Affairs Bureau decided that it should be 120 yuan per day. So far, it has been issued for the seventh week. In the sixth week, the company believed that the number of workers living in the factory had decreased, and insisted that the food expenses be reduced to 80 yuan per day. After detailed investigation by the Social Affairs Bureau, it advised the company to continue to maintain it reluctantly. As a result, all the workers went to the Social Affairs Bureau to petition. The Social Affairs Bureau advised them to temporarily receive 100 yuan per day, or 700 yuan per period. The day before yesterday, the trade union's Xia Zhongzhao accompanied Zhu Guilin of the Social Affairs Bureau to the company to receive the seventh installment of food expenses. The company insisted on only 700 yuan per period and refused to supplement it.

Surrounding Petition: Afterwards, after Xia Zhongzhao of the trade union returned to the factory and reported to the workers, all the workers believed that the meager 160 yuan per day for food expenses was not enough to maintain the lives of more than 1,200 workers. If it was reduced again, it would be tantamount to putting the workers to death. Therefore, at 8:00 a.m. yesterday, more than 250 people automatically gathered and went to the Nanjing Road Sanyou Industrial Society's retail department to petition, demanding (1) that the workers' food expenses be at least 120 yuan per day, and (2) that work be resumed as soon as possible to maintain the workers' livelihood. By 9:00 a.m., they arrived at the retail department and went upstairs. As a result, the shop on the ground floor, the second floor, and the third floor were all crowded. At the door, there was a banner written in bamboo cloth in Chinese and English: "We are fighting for the problem of food, please do not interfere by third parties."

Conflict Occurred: When the workers were petitioning, a special Western detective from the Laozha Police Station passed by and asked if the company had allowed the banner hung at the door. The staff of the retail department replied that it had not been allowed, and it was forced. As a result, the Western detective immediately went to report. Twenty minutes later, the Laozha Police Station dispatched more than 40 Chinese and Western armed detectives to drive away the petitioning workers and ordered them to go to the police station. At that time, the workers agreed to go to the police station as a whole. At that time, the Western detectives suddenly stopped them and drove the workers on the third floor to the second floor, and from the second floor to the shop downstairs. When they arrived downstairs, a conflict occurred between the workers and the police. Suddenly, phlegm, chairs, and orange peel were all weapons, and the order was in chaos. The detectives, seeing the large number of workers, frantically blew the whistle to call for reinforcements.

Traffic Interrupted: At that time, when the workers and police clashed, the Nanjing Road Sanyou retail department was extremely chaotic. Nearby detectives arrived after hearing the alarm. At that time, traffic was interrupted on Nanjing Road from west to Zhejiang Road and east to Fujian Road, and all kinds of vehicles were completely blocked and stopped. It was not until 11:00 a.m. that it returned to its original state.

Arrested Were Released Immediately: During the conflict, seven workers including Luo Ailin were injured. Three glass display windows of the retail department were shattered, and the counter was damaged by squeezing. At that time, three workers were arrested and taken to the police station. Afterwards, all the workers followed. The police, seeing the workers leaving the retail department, immediately closed the iron gate and prohibited the workers from entering and leaving. The arrested were taken to the Laozha Police Station. After questioning by the police chief, the police severely rebuked them, as the workers were first-time offenders and not initiators, and then released them leniently.

Petition to the Municipal Government: Seeing that the iron gate of the retail department was closed, the petitioning workers hired a moving truck and went to the Municipal Government to petition. It was already after 1:00 p.m. At the same time, the workers who remained in the factory went to the Municipal Government after hearing the news, demanding (1) that the food expenses be issued strictly, at 120 yuan per day, and (2) that the murderers be punished. Secretary Wang Shaozhai then ordered the election of representatives Du Shouting, Bao Boyi, Xuan Lihe, Wan Quanfa, Zhang Tingliang, Chen Xinzhi, Gong Huanshan, Wang Xuecui, Qin Changgeng, and Hong Meishuo. Eleven

people went to see him. Regarding the workers' demands, he promised to investigate and deal with them immediately, and notified Wang Xianqing, director of the mediation section of the Social Affairs Bureau, by telephone to rush to persuade and explain everything to the workers' representatives. It was not until 6:30 p.m. that the workers' representatives persuaded the workers to leave first.

Authorities Interrogate: The Social Affairs Bureau has appointed an accountant to audit the factory's closure dispute. In recent days, they have also consulted with the Municipal Party Department and the Municipal Government to find a solution as soon as possible. Yesterday afternoon, when representatives of the Sanyou Industrial Society of the Seventh District Cotton Textile Industry Union were summoned for questioning, Xia Zhongzhao and Qin Haiyan were sent to the office at 3:00 p.m. Director Wang Xianqing of the mediation section happened to be away on his way to the Municipal Government, so Zhu Guilin received them and made a simple inquiry. However, the company's representatives were absent.

Company Statement: The Sanyou Industrial Society issued a statement yesterday, saying that the Sanyou Society's factory was occupied by the Japanese army during the January 28th Incident, and then withdrew on May 31st. On June 2nd, hundreds of workers moved in, demanding resumption of work and relief food. The Municipal Government reluctantly followed the petition, instructing the company to maintain it temporarily and provide appropriate relief. The Social Affairs Bureau, in consultation with the company in June, temporarily gave 120 yuan per day, so 840 yuan was taken away every week. It has been five weeks now. The company has repeatedly received reports that many workers have left the factory automatically because the problem has not been resolved for a long time, and that it has been a long time, which is different from the temporary significance. It requested the Social Affairs Bureau to reduce the payment. After investigation by the Social Affairs Bureau, it contacted the company and changed it to 100 yuan per day. This amount was received last week. The day before yesterday (10th), trade union representatives Xia Zhongzhao, Gong Zishen, and others, together with Social Affairs Bureau representative Zhu Guilin, continued to receive

The 700 yuan went away. Unexpectedly, the next day (11th), hundreds of workers suddenly went to the retail department on Nanjing Road and posted slogans on the glass windows, and were interfered by plainclothes detectives and patrolmen, almost resulting in violence. Three people were then arrested. Afterwards, the manager went to the police station and learned the whole story. As for the arrested workers, the police station, knowing that they were first-time offenders and not initiators, immediately gave them guidance leniently and ordered them not to take such unconscious actions in the future, lest they cause inconvenience. (The trade union also has a declaration to issue, which is omitted here.)

Two Labor-Management Disputes Resolved 156

Fragrance Industry Conditions Signed: After the fragrance industry workers in this city resumed work, the labor-management conditions were mediated by the Labor-Management Mediation Committee at 9:00 a.m. yesterday. After a long period of discussion, the agreement was signed at 12:30 p.m. The original text stated that the parties in the dispute were requesting the improvement of treatment. After being convened for mediation by this committee, the two parties agreed and signed an agreement, which is recorded as follows: (1) The original labor-management conditions remain effective. (2) The wages of workers in both the "Benbang" (local) and "Kebang" (visiting) groups shall be increased by 0.52 yuan per day per person, starting from the 20th of this month. This matter was signed and agreed to by the representatives of both parties. The mediation is established and is regarded as a labor contract between the parties in the dispute.

Jingyi Mediation Established: The Jingyi Leather Factory's old and new factories in Bajiao Bridge, Zhabei, were both destroyed after the war. The factory is now trying to recover. All the workers demanded the resumption of work. Yesterday, after the Social Affairs Bureau mediated, the labor and management stated their reasons. The discussion began immediately and the labor and management agreed and signed to resolve the issue. The record of the settlement is recorded below: (1) The factory recognizes that it will try its best to prepare for the resumption of work and notify the trade union ten

days before the resumption of work, and will give priority to employing old workers. All workers in the old and new factories should work in their original factories. (2) The factory should subsidize the living expenses of all workers remaining in Shanghai at present, at 7 yuan per person, but those who are in debt are allowed to deduct it.

Inquired about the Chinese Political Situation. Wang Xiaolai Clarifies the Erroneous Report in the Japanese Newspaper 160

A reporter from the New Sound News Agency, regarding the report in the Japanese newspaper "Shanghai Mainichi Shimbun" published on the 10th of this month, which stated that the "Blood Soul Exterminate Traitors Corps" was led by Wang Xiaolai, Chairman of the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce, specifically visited Mr. Wang yesterday to inquire about the matter. According to Mr. Wang, he had no knowledge of the corps. The translation of the original report and Mr. Wang's statement are as follows:

Report in the Japanese Newspaper: It roughly stated that a group called the "Blood Soul Exterminate Traitors Corps," which is currently vigorously promoting the boycott of Japanese goods by Chinese merchants through violent intimidation and other inappropriate behaviors, is unexpectedly led by Wang Xiaolai, Chairman of the Chinese Products Joint Association and the General Chamber of Commerce, who is the main figure behind the scenes. Most of the members of the corps are remnants of the Volunteer Army, numbering about fifty to sixty people. This matter has now been definitively confirmed, and there is no doubt about it.

Mr. Wang's Statement: Mr. Wang stated, "On the 26th of last month, I participated in the Shanghai Industrial and Commercial Inspection Group and went to Qingdao for inspection. Along the way, we passed through Weihaiwei and only returned to Shanghai on the evening of the 7th. Before I left Shanghai, I was unaware of the existence of the 'Blood Soul Exterminate Traitors Corps.' When I returned to Shanghai, I saw it in the Shanghai newspapers a few days before the inspection. It is ridiculous that the newspaper claimed that I was the leader of the corps. I have always been open and aboveboard in my actions. If it were something I did, I would never be afraid to admit it. Otherwise, I would definitely not acknowledge it. As for the General Chamber of Commerce advising various trade associations to sever economic ties with Japan, it was based on resolutions passed by successive meetings of member representatives. As the chairman, it is my natural responsibility, along with other executive committee members, to implement the resolutions of the member representatives' meeting, regardless of any difficulties or dangers. This is what I can tell the public."

German Community Celebrates Republic and Constitution Memorial 164

German Consul Unable to Attend Due to Illness. Yesterday was the anniversary of the German Parliament's declaration of the Republican Constitution, also known as the Weimar Constitution. The local German community held its routine celebrations. However, due to the German Consul-General Kerlenburg's ongoing illness, the Consulate General did not hold a meeting to receive congratulations as usual. Only German community groups and clubs held celebrations, all with great excitement. On November 9, 1918, two days after the armistice, Emperor Wilhelm of Germany announced his abdication. Subsequently, the National Assembly took over the government, announced the dissolution of the Parliament, and established a republic. The following January, the Parliament was elected and convened in Weimar on February 6. On February 11, Ebert was elected as the first president. Subsequently, on July 31, the new constitution was drafted and promulgated on August 11, marking the Constitution Memorial Day.

All fishing boats, regardless of their origin, within the jurisdiction of this administration must, within one month from the date of this notice, uniformly comply with the fishing boat management regulations of this administration and apply for fishing boat license plate numbers. In addition to issuing separate orders to various patrol vessels, fishing protection teams, and offices to comply with this order, this notice is hereby issued for general knowledge. All fishing boats must strictly comply with this order and must not wait or delay, lest they be investigated and penalized. This is imperative. Bureau Chief Fan Zhilong.

Local News Two

Heavy Thunderstorm Last Night in Shanghai 168

Beneficial to Farmland, Reduces Plague Atmosphere

The weather in Shanghai has been extremely hot, often around 100 degrees. Due to the drought, many of the rice paddies in the surrounding countryside have withered and yellowed. Farmers have been longing for a heavy rain, but the scorching sun has continued without any sign of rain. Yesterday, from morning to evening, dark clouds gathered and scattered in the sky. In the Nanshi area, there was a heavy rain for a few minutes around 4 PM, but it stopped quickly. Around 9:30 PM, there was a sudden thunderstorm with heavy rain. It lasted for about an hour. Some roads overflowed onto the stone steps because the ditches could not drain the water in time. Although the amount of rainfall was not large, the farmland has been sufficiently moistened. The plague atmosphere in various places can also be reduced by the coolness after the rain.

Garbage Problem in Concessions 169

Accumulated in Longhua Mouth, Land Leased in Chinese Territory

Annual Cleaning Fee of 200,000 Yuan

The garbage problem in the Shanghai concessions has been difficult to solve for a long time. The Public Concession once dumped garbage into the Suzhou River, which aroused opposition from all sides. Later, there was a proposal to melt the garbage with machinery, but it was not realized due to the excessive cost. Recently, negotiations have begun with the Chinese authorities to find suitable open space in the wilderness area of the city for accumulation. It is heard that a piece of land of about 150 acres has been found in the Longhua Mouth area, which can accumulate more than six years of garbage. According to the current estimate, the Chinese territory produces about 400 to 500 tons of garbage per day, the French Concession the same amount, and the British Concession 500 to 700 tons. The garbage is transported by barge to the site for accumulation every day. There are no residents within three or four miles of the site, so there is no impact on hygiene. Moreover, the site is currently a low-lying area, which can be leveled after six years of accumulation. This is a win-win situation. The concession authorities have now decided to pay the municipal government a cleaning tax of 200,000 yuan per year (80,000 yuan for the French Concession and 120,000 yuan for the Public Concession). The Sanitation Bureau will allocate this revenue specifically for garbage disposal, such as building garbage wharves, building garbage barges, garbage trucks, etc. Judging from past circumstances, the municipal government's annual expenditure on garbage disposal is about 80,000 yuan. With the addition of this 200,000 yuan, it can be said that it will be much more convenient to handle sanitation affairs.

Case of Indian Police Killing Chinese 170

Four Witnesses Questioned Yesterday

The trial of five Indian police officers, Sasa Mungen and Aladaite, etc., from the Lizezhongli Guanlong district of Feihong Road in Hongkou, who prevented tenants from moving and stabbed Zhou A'yu to death and injured Yi A'san on the 2nd of this month, was continued yesterday at the British Public Hall. The judge was Haynes. The defendant, the Chinese Business Company, appointed lawyer Levenson to appear in court to defend them. Yesterday, the witnesses Wilson, Zhang Hongyuan, Mao Baifu, and Baden were questioned. The first witness, Wilson, testified that he was an assistant surveyor at the Public Works Department of the Municipal Council and had surveyed Lizezhongli, and presented several maps of the section to the court for reference. The second witness, Zhang Hongyuan, testified that he was an employee of the Huafang Photo Studio at No. 11 Wuhua Road, Zhabei. On the morning of August 3, at 11 AM, he was ordered by the Zhabei police to take photos of the deceased in Lizezhongli. He saw a male Chinese person, approximately 20 years old or older, lying straight on the ground, with blood stains on his body. The photographic negatives submitted to the court were the ones he had taken. As for the location of the corpse on the map, he could not be completely sure, as he did not often go to that area and was not very familiar with the terrain. The third witness, Mao Baifu, testified that he was a photographer at the Public Works Department and had taken several photos of the building addresses and the corpse in Lizezhongli. The photos submitted to the court were the ones he had taken. The fourth witness, Baden, testified that he was a doctor at the British Consulate and had examined the corpse at the Shaoxing Guild Hall in Zhabei on August 5 with forensic doctor Wei Ligong. After opening the coffin, he found that the corpse had decomposed, but he found a clear wound on the chest. He examined the wound and found that it was approximately one inch deep between the fourth and fifth ribs on the left chest. The wound was likely caused by a broad and long knife. The injury was very serious and could have been caused by a forceful thrust by the murderer or a sharp blade. Therefore, even a very healthy person would have died from such an injury. The small steel knife submitted to the court was similar to the murder weapon. After this testimony, the court adjourned. The witnesses Dong Wushi, Hong Erbao, Hong Kaifa, Chen Yaxi, Xu Junchuan, Shi Yanqi, Wang Jinfu, Pan Zhengling, etc., will continue to be questioned today. It will take three or four days to complete the questioning.

Verdict of the Russian Beggar Case 171

Zhou Zongxiang and Two Others Found Not Guilty

Abandoned Leading to Death Not Accepted. The case of the Russian beggar, Qiaoqiladitide Ai'fu, who died in the Second Special District Court Detention Center on June 19, was suspected to have been caused by injuries inflicted by prison guards, according to a report by the corpse examiner, Simon Grantki, who claimed that the beggar was not treated and died. The Police Department prosecuted the warden of the detention center, Xu Chongwen, forensic doctor Yu Minggao, and the prison guard Zhou Zongxiang in the Second Special District Court, accusing them of abandonment leading to death under Article 310, Paragraph 2 of the Criminal Code. After the presiding judge of the Criminal Court, Wang Gang, opened the court for trial, he hired the famous British and French forensic experts Tu Weiliyao and Si Mis, together with the court's forensic doctors Wei Ligong and Xuan Wei, to re-examine the corpse. The result determined that the death was indeed caused by illness. The defendants were defended by five lawyers, Zhao Chen, Liu Shixiong, Shan Yuhua, Li Cishan, and Jiang Yiping. After the closing arguments were concluded, the sentencing was scheduled for 9 AM yesterday. The previous report had already recorded the circumstances. At 9 AM yesterday, the defendants and their lawyers arrived at the court to await instructions. The Police Department was still represented by lawyer Fei Xizhen. At 10 AM, presiding judge Wang and court clerk Fang Mengzhou arrived at Criminal Court One and called the defendants and plaintiffs to the court. After briefly questioning their age, origin, occupation, and address, the verdict was announced. The main text stated, "Zhou Zongxiang, Xu Chongwen, and Yu Minggao are all found not guilty. The part of Zhou Zongxiang's case that involves abandonment leading to death is not accepted. Zhou Zongxiang will remain on bail from his original guarantor. Yu Minggao will be released on bail from his shop guarantor."

Taxpayers' Association Sends Another Letter to the Municipal Council Opposing Telephone Price Increase 172

Public Prosperity Depends on Individual Prosperity

Automatic Telephone Still Difficult to Connect, Are People Satisfied? The Shanghai Concession Taxpayers' Association sent a letter yesterday to the General Office of the Public Concession Municipal Council, stating: "Dear Sirs, we have received a letter from the Shanghai Citizens' Association stating that the Shanghai Telephone Company has increased telephone usage fees from 42 taels to 65 taels per year for residential users and from 78 taels to 105 taels per year for commercial users, effective July 1st of this year, and must be applied retroactively to March 27th of this year. Although the Municipal Council opposed this increase beforehand, it did not respect the opinions of the taxpayers' representative bodies and approved it anyway. The only reason given was that the Municipal Council was bound by the contract signed with the company two years ago and had to follow the Anson report. However, the Municipal Council disregarded the economic depression and the social and economic difficulties, and only cared about the company's profit of 8% plus 2%, totaling 10%, which is unfair. As everyone with legal knowledge knows, the strength of international treaties is stronger than contracts, and the effect of the international debt contract is the same as that of the contract signed by the Municipal Council and the company. When US President Hoover, in view of the world's economic difficulties and at the request of the debtor countries, implemented a one-year moratorium on war debts last year, he was willing to relax the terms of the debt contract. On July 9th of this year, the Lausanne Conference in Europe, under the principle of British Prime Minister MacDonald (Public prosperity depends on individual prosperity), greatly reduced the reparations paid by Germany under the Treaty of Versailles, as determined by Dawes and Young, to only a fraction of Young's number, and stipulated that the bonds would only be issued after three years if business recovered, or never issued within fifteen years, which shows how clear-sighted European and American politicians are (Individual prosperity must be maintained in order to maintain public prosperity). They are willing to change international treaties, but who would believe that the members of the Municipal Council are not aware of this and cannot negotiate a change with the Shanghai Telephone Company? Some say that the only purpose of the Municipal Council is to keep public utility organizations in a particularly advantageous position, and the interests of taxpayers are secondary. The Association does not agree with this, but the price increase of the electricity company, the change of electricity bills from quarterly to monthly, the failure to return two-thirds of the deposit, the price increase of the water company, and the use of water meters, which has increased water bills by more than seven times, show that the Municipal Council has approved the telephone company's request in the same way, just as it did in the autumn of economic depression and market decline. It is difficult to silence those who hold the above view. Your council is the representative body of taxpayers within the concession. We specifically request that you investigate and strive to achieve the goal of canceling the telephone price increase. The above is the reason. In response to this, the Association believes that the reason for the economic downturn is to write to your bureau to express opposition. We are honored to have received a reply stating that the board of directors has considered it, but we are sorry that the results of the consideration have not been shown. As for the opinions of the Citizens' Association, the Association believes that they are very reasonable, but the Association has one more point to add, that is, (press the automatic machine) but it is still not easy to talk to people, whether (performance) can be called (satisfactory), and (not retroactive) is a legal principle, but now it wants to increase prices retroactively to March 27th, The Association agrees with the opinion of the Da Mei Evening News, and there are users who often suffer from poor condition during the two-year repair period. Once they press the automatic machine on March 26th, they want to bear the price increase, and they completely ignore the loss of name but not reality during the two years, which is also not considered in terms of fairness. It is appropriate for the Shanghai Telephone Company to allocate a large amount of money to re-price, and more technicians to rush to press the automatic machine to avoid the punishment of postponement. I deeply understand that what your bureau considers satisfactory is interpreted as (press the automatic machine), not as (full performance). In terms of law, facts and economic conditions, the telephone price increase is really not feasible under the current situation. We should write to your bureau again to consider and negotiate with the company to cancel it, and wait until the performance is complete and the social economy is restored before discussing it again. This is addressed to the General Office of the Shanghai Public Concession Municipal Council.

Public Security Bureau Seeks Lost Boy 174

Song Liufa's House in Huangjia Yan, Liudao Township, Investigated. The Shanghai Public Security Bureau sent a letter to this newspaper yesterday, stating: "Dear Sir, according to the Shanghai County Government's letter No. 206, the report from Zhao Lian, Director of the Second Branch of the Public Security Bureau of this county, states that Yang Hui, a patrol officer from the First Police Station, reported that he had learned on July 3rd that Song Liufa's house in Huangjia Yan, Liudao Township, was hiding a young boy of four years old. The officer immediately led a long police officer to arrest him and found the harboring offender, Song Liufa, and the four-year-old boy at the scene. After a preliminary interrogation, Song Liufa confessed that the boy was sent to his house by his friend, Fu Lou, a master of the Master Fang Xiang Sheng, and that he did not know the details. It was found that the bandit leaders Fang Xiang Sheng, Fu Lou, and Huang Wenxian, etc., all lived in Zhoujiaqiao, Shanghai, and had not been arrested. Fearing that they would escape after hearing the news, the Shanghai County Government was reported to send police to arrest them and bring them back for verification. Based on this, the officer immediately conducted a preliminary interrogation. Song Liufa's confession was roughly the same as the police station's report, but the exact location where the boy was kidnapped could not be determined until Fu Lou and others were arrested and brought to justice. Therefore, the confession was copied and Song Liufa and the boy were sent together for interrogation. At the county level, Song Liufa confessed that the boy was sent by Zhou Yusheng (Fang Xiang Sheng), who lived in the city. The Shanghai Public Security Bureau Sixth District was also contacted to arrest Zhou Yusheng and bring him back for interrogation. At the same time, Zhao Lian, Director of the Second Branch of the Public Security Bureau of this county, was ordered to summon Song Liufa's wife, Song He Shi, to the county for interrogation. After separate interrogations, Zhou Yusheng firmly denied that he had sent a boy to be raised, and Song Liufa and his wife Song He Shi also gave conflicting confessions. Involving a criminal case, in addition to sending Zhou Yusheng, Song Liufa, Song He Shi, and the boy to the Shanghai District Court for investigation, a photo of the boy, whose name and address are unknown, is also sent. Please check the photo and publish it in the news column so that the boy's family can read it and come to claim him. Sincerely, Shanghai Public Security Bureau. A photo is attached."

Raid on an Opium Den in Yü-Ch'ing Lane, Amoy Road 175

An Elderly Man of Sixty Still Engaged in Illegal Activities. Shanghai, a place where people from all corners of the world gather, is a mixture of good and bad. Illegal activities occur in endless succession, such as the sale of opium and distribution of narcotics. Although the National Government's laws explicitly prohibit these and the police conduct strict investigations, these lawless elements still employ cunning tricks to sell them openly. A scoundrel named Wang, residing at No. 206, Lane 4, Yü-Ch'ing Lane, Amoy Road in this city, privately established an opium-selling operation and set up several opium couches for people to smoke, indulging in clouds of smoke. This had been going on for more than a day. Yesterday, the Anti-Narcotics Department of the General Police Station received a tip-off. After repeated secret investigations by detectives, the information was found to be accurate. At 11:00 AM, West District Inspector Pan Ken-sz, along with Chinese Detectives Sung Ping-cheng, Chen Yao-ting, and the entire armed force, drove police vehicles to the address. They apprehended the main suspect, Wang, a woman, and confiscated a small jar of opium paste, three large bags of raw opium, opium pipes, lamps, trays, and a large number of other prohibited items from the residence at No. 206 Yü-Ch'ing Lane. After the search, the detectives temporarily detained the suspects at the Old Zhabei Police Station, pending transfer to the court today for trial. It is said that the internal layout of the opium den was quite sophisticated, and the hiding place for the opium was particularly ingenious. The main suspect, Wang, is nearly sixty years old. It is truly lamentable that he is engaging in such illegal activities at his advanced age.

Special Shipping News 176

Recovery of the Yangtze Wharf. The Yangtze Wharf in Pudong was taken back from German merchants during the European War. Afterwards, the Japanese Ocean Company leased it from the Ministry of Communications of the former Northern Government for a period of five years. After the lease expired, the Japanese company, having made substantial profits, forcibly renewed the lease for another five years with the Ministry of Communications. Even after the second term expired, they were unwilling to return it to China. After the establishment of the National Government, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, through various negotiations, finally regained the wharf from the Japanese. It is now under the management of the Ministry of Communications. However, last year, a Mr. Chen and others organized the China Wharf Company and leased the Yangtze Wharf from the ministry for 200,000 yuan. A contract was signed, but the rent was overdue. The Ministry of Communications has announced the cancellation of the China Company's lease and will seek new tenants for the wharf.

Merchant Ship Loses Anchor in Storm. The various merchant ships chartered by the Ministry of Military Affairs to transport the 19th Route Army to Amoy and other locations have now completed their mission and are beginning to be released. The first ship, "Fairness," has already arrived in Shanghai. The second ship, "Chia-ho," also sailed from Amoy back to Shanghai. According to a telegram from the ship yesterday, it encountered a strong wind shortly after leaving the Amoy sea. It anchored temporarily to avoid the storm, but the wind and waves were too strong, and the anchor chain broke. One of the starboard anchors was lost in the sea, along with ninety feet of iron chain. The "Chia-ho" ship is safe. The lost anchor and chain have been reported to the Amoy Navy for salvage.

Inferior Goods Shipped to North China. The Japanese ship "Hua Shan Maru" departed today for Qingdao, Tianjin, Dalian, and other ports, carrying a large quantity of inferior cloth and Japanese kelp to North China. Yesterday, the ship was docked at the Mitsubishi Wharf, loading these inferior goods for export in significant quantities.

The Hsin-Wei Relief Association Held its Fourth Executive Committee Meeting Yesterday 177

The Hsin-Wei Relief Association of Yunnan Road held its fourth executive committee meeting yesterday afternoon. Attendees included Chu Tzu-chiao, Ch'ü Wen-liu, Chen Ai-shih, Huang Han-chih, Huang Po-tu, and others.
