Bandits Opened Fire on Police During Arrest Attempt on Husi Kaixuan Road 178

Police Sergeant Hsu Kuo-jen of the Second Precinct, Sixth District of the Husi Municipal Police Bureau, along with patrol officers from the Ta-hsi Road Police Station, patrolled back and forth along the K'ai-hsüan Road area, an extraterritorial road, yesterday morning at around 11:00 AM. As they walked in front of the railroad crossing, they noticed shadowy figures whispering to each other. Sergeant Hsu, considering the late hour, determined that they were not good people. He shouted the password and was about to approach for a search when the bandits suddenly opened fire. Sergeant Hsu immediately ordered the officers to crouch on the ground and return fire. The number of bandits continued to grow, reaching about twenty or more, and they surrounded the four police officers. Fortunately, Patrol Inspector Chang Chung-te of the station and Police Sergeant Chou Yi-ta of the Fa-hua Police Station heard the gunshots and led officers from all directions to surround the area. A fierce gun battle ensued, with bullets raining down. The two sides exchanged fire for about a hundred rounds over approximately forty minutes. Realizing they were outnumbered, the bandits began to flee north. The patrol officers pursued them, but lost them near the Fan-wang-tu Bridge on Chung-shan Road due to the darkness. They returned to the station to report the situation and await further investigation.

Landlord Forcing Tenant to Death in Pudong 179

Causing Public Outrage. Various Labor Unions Petition Authorities for Strict Punishment of Landlords. The petition requests justice in the matter of landlords coercing human lives. The unions recently received a report from Widow Lu Hu of No. 12, Stone Bridge, Muddy Ford, Pudong, stating that while her husband was alive, he had rented the house from landlord Ku Lung-lung for nearly twenty years. On May 16, 1930, her husband, Ming-chung, was forced to commit suicide by poison due to a debt dispute with Ku Lung-lung. Everyone knew about this. At the time, the landlord asked someone to intercede, pleading to avoid prosecution. The widow, being a woman, was both intimidated by his power and limited by her financial situation. She harbored a great grievance but did not dare to speak out. Her family of six depended entirely on her husband to support them. After his death, the family's circumstances gradually deteriorated. They lacked sufficient food, and the monthly rent relied entirely on her borrowing from all sides. Since last year, their livelihood has become increasingly difficult, and debts have piled up, making it impossible to pay the rent. This year, they have been affected by the war, frequently facing food shortages, and are even less able to cover the accumulated rent. Landlord Ku Lung-lung disregarded their old friendship and forced them to move out. The widow begged for leniency, promising to find a new place to move within seven weeks. She found a house owned by Ku Ah-san, preparing to move there. Unexpectedly, the new landlord and Ku Lung-lung were relatives. Ku Lung-lung secretly sabotaged the arrangement, claiming that the house had already been rented to someone else, and returned the deposit of three yuan after three days of negotiations. She tried to find another house, but it was difficult to find a suitable location in a short time. The widow searched all day in the heat, exhausted. Landlord Ku Lung-lung showed no sympathy and came to her house yesterday afternoon, demanding that she move out immediately, and verbally abused the widow unreasonably. The neighbors witnessed this and felt indignant. The widow, unable to bear the coercion and humiliation, attempted suicide that evening. She was discovered, but it was too late to save her. Alas, within two years, both her husband and her mother-in-law were forced to death by the landlord. Ku Lung-lung relies on his wealth and believes he can manipulate everything. What difficulty would there be in escaping punishment for these mere human lives? Her husband's revenge has not been taken, and now another grievance arises from her mother-in-law's death. If this injustice is not redressed, how can she bear to continue living in this world? Therefore, she cries out to the association to uphold justice and provide assistance. Both the deceased and the living will be grateful. The unions have previously filed a case regarding disputes over rent reduction. Now, the landlord Ku Lung-lung, relying on his property rights, oppresses the widowed and helpless, resulting in two major tragedies. People are not made of wood or stone; who would not be outraged upon hearing this? In order to uphold humanity and protect human rights, the unions cannot stand idly by in the face of this situation. Therefore, they report the facts and petition the association to immediately punish the landlord according to the law for the crime of relying on wealth to coerce human lives, thereby preventing further illegal acts and comforting the souls of the wronged. After receiving the weeping plea for assistance from the tenant Lu Hu, the Pudong Rent Reduction Association immediately dispatched Cheng Hsieh-cheng, Chang Tzu-ping, Sung Pei-chi, Liu Hai-ju, and four others to investigate. That evening, they convened an emergency meeting to discuss assistance measures. They decided to (1) issue a declaration; (2) petition higher authorities to uphold justice and quickly revise rent reduction standards to prevent future tragedies; (3) inform tenants, based on the notice from the Municipal Rent Reduction Association and the resolution of the joint meeting of various organizations on August 6, that they should temporarily postpone rent payments until the central government reviews and revises the standards; and (4) issue a declaration supporting the Municipal Party Committee's rent reduction efforts.

Bandits Who Opened Fire on Police During Arrest Attempt Sentenced to Ten Years in Prison 180

The bandit Li Chin-sheng, from Yangchow, was found to have conspired with accomplices to rob the home of Lin Chao-lin at No. 824 Wuchang Road at midnight on March 1st of this year. They stole valuables worth over 500 yuan and opened fire on police during the arrest attempt. As a result, he was apprehended by Chinese Detective Liu Te-cheng and Chinese Constable No. 3072 of the Hongkou Police Station. Li was also seriously injured. He was handed over to the First Special District Court. The various details of his repeated interrogations and confessions have been reported in this newspaper. The case has been concluded and is awaiting sentencing. Yesterday morning, Judge Shen Ping-rong presided over the Fourth Criminal Division and sentenced Li Chin-sheng to ten years of imprisonment. The number of days he was detained before the sentence was finalized will be credited at a rate of two days of detention for one day of imprisonment. One automatic pistol, four bullets, and one shell casing were all confiscated.

News from Various Trade Associations 181

Marine Products and Grocery Trade: The Marine Products and Grocery Trade Association originally had over sixty members. Since the September 18th Incident, due to the impact of the boycott of Japanese goods, nearly half of them have closed down. Of the remaining thirty or so, seven or eight are in the process of liquidation due to financial difficulties. The majority of the rest are engaged in domestic marine products, Sichuan-Hankou groceries, or Western goods. Unexpectedly, at this precarious time, the association received a letter from the Ten-Man National Salvation Group. The association urgently convened an emergency meeting of all members yesterday. After deliberation, everyone agreed that the Tung-sheng firm mentioned in the group's letter was indeed a member of the Shanghai Marine Products Trade Association and not something that the association could overstep its authority to address. The Tung-hui firm has already closed down, making it impossible to investigate. However, the Chen-ta, Shun-cheng, Heng-shun, and Hsieh-chang firms should be ordered to provide truthful written responses within two days. At the same time, member trades were urgently notified to fill out voluntary statements. The association will hire investigators to conduct investigations at any time. If any member is found to be selling enemy goods secretly, after the association verifies the evidence, their market license will be revoked, and their crimes will be announced in the newspaper in order to thoroughly implement the association's policy of perpetual economic severance with Japan. The emergency notice reads: "Concerning the urgent notice, based on a letter from the Ten-Man National Salvation Group, etc., it has been investigated that Tung-sheng firm is a member of the Marine Products Trade Association, and Tung-hui firm has already closed down, so there is no need to discuss it. The Chen-ta and other four firms have already been decided by the general meeting to provide truthful written responses. All other members should fill out voluntary statements and submit them to the association. If any member is found to be selling enemy goods secretly, after the association verifies the evidence, their market license will be revoked, and their crimes will be announced in the newspaper in order to warn others. It is hoped that all members will conduct themselves properly. Regarding the sale of enemy goods, correct them if they exist, and work harder if they do not. Otherwise, if danger occurs, it will be too late for regret. Please make an effort to act accordingly. A voluntary statement form is issued to be filled out and returned as required. This is specially notified."

Bamboo Shoot Trade: The Bamboo Shoot Trade Association held its inaugural meeting at the Mei-yuan firm on Tou-shih Street at 2:00 PM the day before yesterday. Twenty-one members attended. Ku Chen-min was publicly elected as the temporary chairman. Representatives Chang Ta-fu from the Shanghai Special Municipal Party Headquarters, Sung Chung-ch'ing from the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau, and Yuan Hung-chun from the Municipal Chamber of Commerce attended the meeting to provide guidance. The chairman first reported on the purpose of the meeting and the preparations made. The articles of association were then discussed one by one and passed without any objections. It was also resolved that (1) the membership fee for new members would be 300 yuan per firm; (2) the regular membership fee would be 2 yuan per person per month; (3) the number of executive committee members would be seven. Under the supervision of representatives from various higher-level bodies, ballots were cast, and the elected executive committee members were Ku Chen-min (20 votes), Tung Kuei-fang (20 votes), Chang Tzu-fan (19 votes), Pao Ta-yuan (19 votes), Lu Sui-ch'ing (18 votes), Chen Sheng-tsai (18 votes), and Tung Yu-ch'ing (18 votes). The alternates were Hsu An-hua (7 votes) and Tung Po-sheng (5 votes). After the meeting, the first executive committee meeting was held, and Ku Chen-min, Chang Tzu-fan, and Tung Kuei-fang were elected as standing committee members. Pao Ta-yuan and Chen Sheng-tsai were elected as investigation committee members. Ku Chen-min was publicly elected as chairman. Department Store Trade: The Department Store Trade Association held its re-election meeting at its headquarters on Sze-ching Road the day before yesterday. Representatives Wang Man-yun from the Municipal Party Headquarters, Hu Yu-ch'i from the Social Affairs Bureau, and Sun Ming-ch'i from the Municipal Chamber of Commerce attended the meeting as scheduled. The presidium included Cheng Hai-jo, Chang Wei, Wang Wei-ying, Ke Yu-yuan, and Chen Hui-ch'ing. (1) An emergency proposal was made to increase the number of supervisory committee members. It was resolved to increase the number to seven. Representatives from the Social Affairs Bureau then drew lots to determine the outgoing committee members: Cheng Hai-jo, Ch'ien Lien-yuan, Cheng Cheng-ch'ing, Ke Yu-yuan, Chang Wei, Wang Pei-fu, and Chang Heng-hai. The remaining committee members were Chen Hui-ch'ing, Chang Li-hsing, Wang Wei-ying, Chen Ping-hsia, Cheng Kuei-chu, Chao Chang-sheng, Chang Shao-chai, and Chin Ping-lan. Next, the executive and supervisory committee members were elected. Wu Yun-ch'ing, Liu Shih-yin, Tan Hui-sheng, Shen Shun-hsiang, Li He-ling, Sung Mao-ch'ing, Sun Cheng-fu, and others were elected as executive committee members. Chen Hsi-sheng, Chu Chin-fu, Chang Shou-chih, Shih Tung-shan, and others were alternates. Cheng Hai-jo, Ch'ien Lien-yuan, Chang Wei, Wang Pei-fu, Ke Yu-yuan, Cheng Cheng-ch'ing, Chu K'ung-liang, and others were elected as supervisory committee members. Hu Yun-fei, Cheng Hai-hsing, Huang Chu-ju, and others were alternates. They were sworn into office on the spot. The meeting then discussed (1) the proposal to promote domestic goods. It was resolved to approve it in principle and to task the executive committee with implementing it. (2) The proposal to boycott enemy goods. It was resolved that (A) Japanese goods would be sealed and sold by the association with its seal. Any goods without the seal would be considered privately imported Japanese goods, and the association would request social sanctions to be enacted and announced in the newspapers; (B) an inspection team would be organized, dispatched by the committee on a rotating basis, to inspect the purchasing ledgers and goods of various stores. Refusal to allow inspection or the discovery of secretly imported Japanese goods would also be announced to the public, requesting public sanctions; (C) there would be rewards for confidential reports. A public announcement would be made regularly in the newspapers. If anyone from any sector of society discovers that a member of the association is secretly importing Japanese goods and reports it to the association, they would be rewarded; (D) the proposal to establish a department store trade center. It was resolved to approve it in principle and to task the executive committee with implementing it; (E) the proposal to establish trade regulations. It was resolved to task the executive committee with drafting them and then convening a general meeting for approval.

Miscellaneous Grains and Oil Cakes Trade: The Miscellaneous Grains and Oil Cakes Association convened a meeting of its members yesterday afternoon, chaired by Tsai Yu-k'un, to thoroughly investigate the sales of Japanese rice by its members, including Tung-hsing-tai and Jen-tai-san firms. The chairman reported that since the incident in the Eastern Provinces, the association had convened a meeting of its members, severed economic ties with Japan, and prohibited the use of Japanese ships. Fearing that members might engage in private buying and selling, the executive committee convened a special meeting in May of this year and resolved to resist to the death and never trade with Japan. If any member violated this resolution, upon discovery, they would be expelled from the association, barred from operating in the market, and the market would be notified. Recently, it was discovered that Tung-hsing-tai was selling Japanese rice. The association sent a letter to the firm, requesting a report on the ship that transported the rice, the date of arrival, and the details of the amount. The firm replied promptly. The rice stored in various warehouses was examined by the public, and it was found that the shipping details reported for three lots did not match the arrival date. This matter is currently under investigation. Suddenly, a letter was received from the North Office of the Bean and Rice Trade, requesting an investigation into Jen-tai-san's exclusive sale of Japanese rice. At the previous meeting, the undersigned was assigned to work with Committee Member Chiang Hung-bin of the Bean and Rice Trade Association and the North Office to investigate the firm. Unexpectedly, the next day, an advertisement was published in various newspapers stating that the Rice Shop Trade Association had sent personnel to investigate the Jen-tai-san, San-tai, and Kai-tai rice shops. They also inspected the books of Jen-tai-san firm, which showed no exclusive sales of Japanese rice, proving everything. However, yesterday a letter was received from the Blood Soul Extermination Group and others, stating that the treacherous merchants Tung-hsing-tai and Jen-tai-san were selling Japanese rice, requesting a thorough investigation, and a letter was received from the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, instructing a warning to be given to colleagues to quickly stop selling Japanese goods. The letters were presented to the members for review and a discussion of measures. After discussion, it was decided that since the Municipal Chamber of Commerce had already organized an investigation team, a letter should be sent immediately requesting the Municipal Chamber of Commerce to send personnel to the meeting. This association will send personnel to thoroughly investigate Tung-hsing-tai, Jen-tai-san, and other firms, and members are warned not to trade with Japan again. If they violate this, they will be severely punished. If members wish to trade goods, they must register with the association, regardless of the goods, in order to facilitate investigation. The meeting adjourned at 6:00 PM.

Clock and Watch Trade: Clock and watch shops, such as Chung-mei and Chung-fa, had already received warnings. Yi-cheng and Sun-kuang-hsing recently received warnings. Upon hearing this news, the Clock and Watch Trade Association sent Secretary Yu Shih-fo to investigate. According to Yu Shih-fo, after thoroughly checking the accounts, there were no new imports. However, upon inspecting the display windows, items were displayed. It is suspected that these were old sealed goods that were privately unsealed and sold. The Extermination Group saw them on display and suspected they were new imports. It is heard that the trade association has replied, ordering the firms to reseal the goods.

French General Police Station West Detective Xia Cai'er and Chinese and Western detectives from the Gambling Raid Squad raided a large roulette gambling den at No. 809 Rue Ghisi. Two Legal Wives 184

It's Always Hard for the Husband. Chang Ta-pao, a native of Yangzhou, is 35 years old. He runs a knitting machine factory on Huei-ning Road in Shanghai. In 1929, following his parents' orders and the words of a matchmaker, he married a woman named Xie (currently 28 years old) in his hometown of Yangzhou. After the wedding, Chang did not bring Xie to Shanghai, leaving her at home to help his parents with farming. The following year (1930), they had a son, who sadly passed away this spring. Xie repeatedly sent letters to Shanghai, but her husband did not return home. Therefore, last month, she took a ship to Shanghai from her hometown. After arriving at the factory, she saw that her husband had another woman. This woman claimed to be Chang Ta-pao's wife, and her husband echoed her claim. As a result, the couple often argued. The day before yesterday, an argument broke out over a trivial matter. Chang and his concubine beat Xie, kicking and punching her, and drove her out of the house. Xie had no choice but to go to her brother, Xie Shun-chi, who runs a tailor shop, Xie Shun-hsing, near the entrance of Hsi-hu Lane on Hsi-men Road in the French Concession, and complained about her husband and his concubine beating her. That evening, Xie took his wife and accompanied his sister back to Wang Ta-pao's factory, intending to ask Chang a few questions. Unexpectedly, Chang's concubine, preempting them, disheveled her hair. When Xie led his sister into the factory, she started to fight Xie without asking the circumstances, claiming that she was also a legal wife. The neighbors, seeing this, felt great indignation and called the police. The police took everyone to the Huei-ning Road police station in the Second District. The patrol officer, after asking the details, advised both parties to leave and let their elders mediate the family matter. Xie and his sister left the police station as instructed. However, Chang's concubine dared to fight Xie again on the way. The patrol officer witnessed the situation and summoned all the witnesses back to the district headquarters (Second District Headquarters). The chief briefly questioned them and then sent the case to the Procuratorate of the District Court for investigation. Yesterday morning, the prosecutor held a preliminary hearing, repeatedly advising Xie that if she wanted to sue her husband, she would have to file a lawsuit in the civil court. The prosecutor then released Chang Ta-pao and his concubine, ordering them to mediate the matter. After leaving, Xie hired a lawyer to draft a complaint to the Shanghai District Court, accusing her husband of abandoning his legal wife.

Protesting the Exclusion of Chinese Goods by Dutch Merchants 186

Two national goods organizations telegraphed Consul Song, urging him to vigorously fight for the Shanghai citizens' advocacy of national goods association and the China National Goods Maintenance Association. Previously, the Philips Company, using the alleged patent for the vacuum pumping method of glass tubes, illegally encroached on the South Seas sales of light bulbs from the Yapuer Electric Factory, affecting the entire problem of overseas trade of national goods manufactured by foreign machines. They have already telegraphed the Consul General in Java, the Batavia Chinese Chamber of Commerce, the Central Party Headquarters, the National Government, the Executive Yuan, the Ministries of Foreign Affairs and Overseas Affairs, and the Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission, requesting them to argue based on reason, protect according to law, and also send letters to the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce and the Overseas Chinese Federation to assist in safeguarding national goods. Yesterday, they again telegraphed Consul Song in Java, stating the advantages and disadvantages and applying for a vigorous fight to maintain overseas trade of national goods. The original telegram reads: "To Song Jun, Consul General of the Republic of China in Batavia, Java: The situation of the Dutch merchant Philips light bulb company repeatedly excluding the national goods light bulbs of the China Yapuer Electric Factory has been detailed in the previous telegram. We believe that due to years of internal strife in our country, industry and commerce have declined, and the economy is in panic. The great powers are taking the opportunity to invade, and if economic invasion is not enough, they follow it up with force. Our country submits to adversity and is unable to resist. The great powers, therefore, regard us as turtles in a jar, doing whatever they want. For example, the Dutch merchant Philips company excludes Yapuer light bulbs, first preventing the sale of its Half bulbs. Seeing that we have no reaction, they take a further step to completely defeat us. This is not a matter of one day's deliberation. The reason why they are proceeding step by step is to test the strength of the unity of our people. They are not afraid of us, but they are sincerely afraid that if our people are united, it will affect the sales of their goods in China. Since they know that our people still hold the stubborn old idea of each sweeping the snow from their own door, they abandon the normal path of commercial warfare and do not hesitate to use this despicable means as a shortcut to defeat Chinese goods. We fear that soon after Yapuer light bulbs, those who are excluded will follow one after another. Is the future of our country's overseas trade and the source of livelihood for overseas Chinese still worth imagining? Yapuer light bulbs are one of the products of the factory, and also one of the national goods of our country. Sales in Java are part of the business of the Yapuer factory, and also part of our country's overseas trade of national goods. The loss is not much, as insignificant as a hair of nine oxen. However, the ambition of foreigners to invade will increase inch by inch and never stop. Looking ahead, the worries are very serious. Therefore, we telegraph again to state the advantages and disadvantages, and sincerely hope that you will fight for it according to reason. It is not too late to mend the fold after the sheep is lost. We beg you to review and verify, and if you grant our request, it will be for the public convenience. Wang Jie'an, Wang Hanqiang, and Wang Xingyi, Standing Committee Members of the China National Goods Maintenance Association, Yu Hede, Feng Shaoshan, Chen Yiting, Chen Binghui, Fang Jiange, Xu Chengru, and Zhang Dezai, Standing Committee Members of the Shanghai Citizens' Advocacy of National Goods Association, kowtow in unison."

Xia Xiuqing's firewood shop in Liuliqiao, Pudong, monopolized the rice straw business. Sun claimed that Wang Laosan went to extort and kill people, and he was cooking dinner at home and knew nothing about it. There was no evidence to the contrary. Old Woman Falls and Dies While Cooling Off 191

Verification Shows Suffocation Due to Stroke. Around 8 pm the night before last, an old woman on Laoyingpanqian, South Shanghai, was holding a palm-leaf fan and walking back and forth to cool off. Unexpectedly, she stumbled forward and fell to the ground, dying immediately. The woman was about fifty years old, wearing short blue cloth shirt and pants, and very obese. Yesterday, Zhang Hongxun, the local bailiff of the Sixth Tu, reported to the local court for verification. Prosecutor Wu and others came to verify and confirmed that she died of suffocation due to a stroke. He ordered the hall to collect the body and wait for someone to claim it.

Iron Factory Owner's Extortion Case 192

Continued Hearing Concluded

Qiu Xianrong Allowed to be Released. Peisheng Iron Factory, No. 734 Zhoujiazui Road, is opened by Chen Zhisheng, a native of Yong. Between the 26th of last month and the 3rd of this month, he received several threatening letters under the name of the Preparatory Committee of the Third Route Seventh Group of the Chinese Communist Party, demanding 100,000 yuan and asking him to publish a lost declaration advertisement in the News, indicating his willingness, with one yuan as a secret code of one thousand yuan, and agreeing to hand over the money near the Shunxintang Opium戒烟 Institute at No. 3 Hua'anfang, North Zhejiang Road. The Huishan Patrol Room was informed and sent Chinese detectives Qi Mengqing, Xu Bingnan, and Shen Binkui to arrest Ye Wu, a Yong woman, and a suspect named Qiu Xianrong, a Lu native in his seventies, at 3:15 pm on the 3rd of this month and escort them to the First Special District Court for interrogation. This has been recorded in this newspaper. Yesterday morning, Judge Chuan Lin conducted a continued interrogation in the Fourth Criminal Court. The patrol room's lawyer Zhang Tianyin stated that during the postponement, the victim received two more signed letters, one saying that the money should be delivered quickly, otherwise he would be shot with Brown Lin bullets, and the money should be sent to Zhou Zhenli or a Yang surnamed person at No. 516 Hengfeng Road, Zhabei. Patrol Room detectives went to investigate and found no such person. The second letter said, "You are not doing things properly, relying on the power of the Patrol Room. Now send the money in silver dollars or banknotes to the same place. If you report to the Patrol Room again, your whole family will be killed," etc. He presented the two letters for inspection and stated that the mastermind of the case was Shi Laisheng, also known as A'er, the lover of the defendant Wu. The two letters were undoubtedly sent by him. The patrol room's investigation clarified that the second defendant, Qiu Xianrong, was not related to the case. He asked him to write and compared the handwriting, which was different. Therefore, he asked to release him first. Then, the victim Chen Zhisheng reported the situation of receiving the letter and publishing the advertisement. He questioned Ye Wu, who admitted to having known Shi Laisheng before, but had canceled it. She firmly stated that she did not know the details of the matter. At that time, Shi gave her a note asking her to go to Qiu Xianrong, that is, A'tai, to pick up a package containing ten yuan. She did not deliver it. Later, she met Patrol Room detectives on the way and gave the paper package to Shi, saying that there were only eight yuan in it. She said that the small number could be discussed with Shi tomorrow and showed the note written by Shi. She did not hear that there were 8,000 yuan in the package, etc. Detective Xu Bingnan also stated that he said those words to her at the time, and took her note, but she snatched the note twice, causing it to be torn. Judge Chuan thoroughly questioned her, and she insisted on her statement, saying that she was indeed fooled by Shi and begged for consideration. The court appointed a lawyer to defend her for free and ordered her to be sent back to custody to await a scheduled verdict. Qiu Xianrong was allowed to be released.

The epidemic is rampant. Some time ago, I introduced the water disinfection method of bleaching powder to the Chinese people, but because some people still have some doubts about it, please publish the attached letter in your newspaper to dispel the doubts of the public. I am very grateful. Please accept the seal of Doctor Zhu Yanggao, the chief writer of the Shenbao Museum. Some people suspect that the drinking water disinfection method introduced by me using bleaching powder is poisonous, and some see that it cannot kill other animal insects in the water (such as mosquito larvae, commonly known as Dahanchong). It is not known that germs are plants, and the effect of bleaching powder is limited to germs, so it does not kill small animals, which is enough to show that it is harmless to animals, and even more harmless to humans. Therefore, I do not hesitate to repeat, please use it, check it, and I am willing to be responsible for the introduction, because the method is simple and effective, cheap and easy to obtain. Attached are a few points on bleaching powder disinfection and other prevention methods: (1) Water and drinking water disinfection: The water in all rivers contains a lot of epidemic bacteria. After it is drawn, it must be disinfected before it can be drunk. Disinfection method: Use half a copper coin's worth of bleaching powder, equal to 0.8 grams, or two and a half cents of the balance, and add it to four洋油箱 kerosene tanks, equal to 80 liters of river water. After 20 hours, all kinds of epidemic bacteria in the water will be killed. Then use this water to wash food utensils, such as bowls, chopsticks, and spoons, and use this water for washing face, gargling, bathing, etc., which can definitely avoid epidemics. It is important not to use the water in the river directly. (2) All food and all utensils for storing food must be covered with gauze to prevent mosquitoes and flies from flying in, because mosquitoes and flies are the media for epidemics. (3) Injecting preventive injections. (4) Do not eat water fruits. If you must eat them, no matter what kind of water fruit, soak them in boiling water for one minute to disinfect them. The above four items are the key points of epidemic prevention, which are easy to implement, and bleaching powder is very cheap, so it is easy for both the rich and the poor to buy and prepare, and the effect is great. I hope that those who live at home should pay attention to this and do not be afraid of trouble, and spread it widely, so that the epidemic can be prevented. Preface

Expulsion of Students Studying in Japan 205

— Buddha

Japan's exclusion of Chinese people is extremely harsh. First, it prohibits laborers from entering the country, then rejects peddlers and merchants, and recently, even students studying abroad are being expelled. In the past week, a student studying in Japan, Tian Xiangfan, was ordered to be deported by the Japanese authorities. Recently, Xu Yulin, a student from Wenzhou, Zhejiang, was prevented from landing in Yokohama, Japan, and was forced to board the Asama Maru and deported. This is a deserved retribution.

No matter who it is, if they have any conscience and a bit of humanity, they would not want to go to Zhabei or Hongkou, because the various cruel images left by the Japanese are vivid in people's minds and unpleasant to see. Moreover, regarding the situation in the Northeast, the Japanese have appointed Mutō as commander of the Kwantung Army to fully realize the plan for unified aggression, and the situation in Jehol is extremely serious. Originally, Chinese students studying in Japan, under these circumstances, unless they are completely heartless, should voluntarily return home. Now, there are still people going to study in Japan, which is truly deserving of the label of cold-blooded, country-humiliating youth. I can only curse a few times like a tram driver ("Pig!"), what else can I say?

However, according to a survey by a certain newspaper the other day, although the number of students going to Japan to study after the September 18th Incident has decreased slightly compared to before, there are still quite a few people going. I don't know what these people think when they step on the land of imperialists, and what face they have when they see imperialists. Mencius said, "What distinguishes humans from animals is only a little bit, and it is nothing more than a sense of shame." If people have no sense of shame, they are worse than animals. Even if these heartless students return home after completing their studies in the future, they will only be a few more Zhao Xinbos, etc., and what will they have to do with our country?

Someone might say, "Buddhists say, 'If you don't enter the tiger's den, how can you get the tiger cubs?' We only know the strength of Japan now, but we don't know why Japan is strong, so we must study in Japan to investigate its content in order to prepare for our future revenge." This saying is also a thank you. Since the late Qing Dynasty's reform, countless people have gone to study in Japan every year. Where is our country strong now? What is the method to deal with Japan? Now, (clutching at straws) it is even more out of the question.

Therefore, these students studying in Japan are not only looked down upon by our countrymen, but even the Japanese find them disgusting, so they say, "Please go back, no need to come."

Science

The Study of Sound 208

— Meng Fu

In the science section of this publication, most of the articles published are about chemical knowledge applied in industry, and there is little research on physics. Therefore, I specially contribute to you some common knowledge about sound in physics.

Sound (Sound), except for those whose hearing organs are damaged, everyone can hear it. It seems that there is nothing surprising, but let's ask how sound is made? How can we hear the sound? What is an echo? And what about all other questions? If you can't answer these, then please patiently read the following!

When the bell rings, we hear the sound. When it has just finished ringing, try to lightly touch the edge of the bell with your lips, and you will feel that the bell is vibrating very violently. Therefore, the success of sound is due to the vibration of objects, and this vibration force is transmitted layer by layer to the place where the sound is received - our ears. Of course, if the ears are covered, the sound will be reduced.

The transmission of sound depends entirely on the air that fills the earth and is everywhere. Now, let's take an experiment: put an alarm clock in a glass cover. At this time, you can clearly hear its ringing. Then, use an air pump to pump out the air in the cover to make it a vacuum, then you can't hear anything. Therefore, when talking on high mountains or airplanes, the sound is very weak, which is because the air is thin at high altitudes.

In addition to air, solids and liquids can also transmit sound, and they are better than air. Here are a few very common examples: stick your ear to the steel rail, and you can hear the sound of a train moving from a long distance. Lie your ear on the table and tap the table with your hand, and the sound will sound much louder than if you don't lie on the table. These are enough to prove that solids can transmit sound. People diving in the water can hear the sound of ships sailing and all kinds of objects hitting in the water from a long distance. This can also prove that liquids can transmit sound.

If there is an obstacle in front of the sound source, the sound will immediately bounce back, which will create an echo. If the distance is close, the echo and the original sound are mixed together, so there is no echo, but the original sound can be increased because of this. This is called reinforcement. Echoes are very detrimental to theaters or venues, because they can hinder and disrupt the audience's hearing. There are also ways to avoid echoes, just place more sound-absorbing materials, such as heavy felt curtains and silk cloth curtains. As for the speed of sound, it is probably slower than light. For example, when it thunders, you always see the lightning first, and then hear the thunder. When firing a cannon, you also see the light and smoke first, and then hear the sound of the cannon. The speed of light is about 138,000 feet per second (equivalent to 650 million Chinese feet), which is more than 5,000 times faster than sound. At 0 degrees Celsius and 76 meters of pressure, the speed of sound is 1,087 feet per second (331 meters). The increase in the speed of sound is directly proportional to the temperature. For every degree the temperature increases, the speed of sound increases by 2 feet. It can generally be remembered that at 20 degrees Celsius (68 degrees Fahrenheit), the speed of sound is 1,130 feet per second. From this, the distance of the sound source can also be inferred from the sound of the cannon, as long as the time elapsed from the light to the sound is multiplied by the speed of sound, and the result is the distance between the sound source and the sound receiver. During the European War, this method was used to calculate the distance and counterattack, but later smokeless gunpowder was used, which made it impossible for the enemy to speculate.

I have mentioned above that solids and liquids transmit sound faster than air. The speed of sound in solids is 15 times faster than in air, and in liquids it is 4.5 times faster. Doesn't it seem that there is nothing surprising about sound, but when you study it, don't you find it very wonderful?

Society Improvement Discussion Group

Proposal to Improve Children's Clothing 209

— Zu'e

We have already discussed the improvement of adult clothing several times in this association, but it is regrettable that we have not paid attention to children's clothing. I think that our country has always paid little attention to children's lives, and the improvement of clothing is particularly lacking. Following the old ways has a great impact on children's development, so I propose to improve children's clothing. I sincerely hope that comrades will contribute to this.

Looking at children's clothing in our country, there is no new design. They only follow the clothing of adults, so that a lively child is often restricted by clothing, which limits their innocence. For example, a boy wearing wide-sleeved robes and loose belts, this kind of dragging appearance is enough for the child to show a dull appearance, and he won't be lively. There are also girls who don't know anything about curves, but adults insist on making them tight-fitting cheongsams, thinking that they are showing the child's fashion, but they don't know that the child's body is being bound. There is also a hard high collar around the head and neck, which is no different from calling her to wear a yoke! So it will only create a gentle and refined child, which is not pitiful?

Originally, clothes are for protecting the body, for oneself and not for others. Only seeking to balance cold and warmth, cleanliness and hygiene is enough. Children don't have much perception, and there is no need to pursue sophistication or fashion at all. We should pay attention to the child's development or whether there are any obstacles. As far as I can see, I will briefly describe the standards of children's clothing as follows:

(1) Lively and Unrestricted: Children have lively innocence, which has a great impact on development and thinking. Wearing adult clothing can limit their liveliness, which is a great drawback. Therefore, children's clothing should be improved to be lightweight and simple, not only should it not bind the body, but also increase their lively spirit through improved clothing.

(2) Simplicity: Simple clothing can cultivate a non-extravagant habit, and children need to jump and run, simple clothes are more durable than gorgeous ones.

(3) Domestic Clothing Materials: The inferior root of despising domestic goods and loving imported goods is very common among Chinese people. Some even deceive their children by making them wear foreign clothes or buying foreign toys because they are noisy, which makes the children plant these inferior roots. How sad! Therefore, children's clothing must strive for domestic products to cultivate a prejudice against not despising domestic goods.

(4) Saving Labor and Materials: Children's clothing must strive to save labor and materials, and the style should be simple. Some densely arranged buttons and other complicated tailoring not only waste clothing materials, but also take a lot of effort, and are inconvenient for children to wear.

(5) Heroic Clothing: Flattering clothing can indeed please people, but it is not as impressive as heroic clothing. In addition to the above improvement standards, the style of children's clothing should also have a heroic spirit. Wearing a small military uniform or a navy suit can give children a brave spirit, which may be helpful for the future of the nation.

These are just a few standards for improvement. Naturally, I have not exhausted all aspects of improvement, especially the implementation of how to improve, which I have not mentioned. I hope that those who are interested will discuss these issues.

February 18

The maid, A Xiang, secretly told me while tidying my room, "The master has found someone for the young lady." A Xiang is a very clever girl. Shanghai Second Special District Court 213

Criminal Judgements:

Police Department versus Zhong Yu Shi, et al., an opium case (Judgement): Zhong Yu Shi is sentenced to six months of imprisonment for providing premises for others to use opium. Zhou Caigui and Lu Lanqing are each sentenced to one month of imprisonment for using opium. The number of days of detention before the judgement is confirmed shall be deducted from the imprisonment at a rate of two days of detention for one day of imprisonment. Lu Lanqing is granted a two-year suspended sentence. The opium paraphernalia is confiscated and destroyed.

▲Police Department versus Zhou Chengsan, et al., an opium case (Judgement): Zhou Chengsan is sentenced to three months of imprisonment for assisting in providing premises for others to use opium substitutes. Yu A'er is sentenced to one month of imprisonment for using opium substitutes. The number of days of detention before the judgement is confirmed shall be deducted from the imprisonment at a rate of two days of detention for one day of imprisonment. The opium paraphernalia is confiscated and destroyed.

▲Police Department versus Song Sihai, et al., an opium case (Judgement): Song Sihai is sentenced to six months of imprisonment for providing premises for others to use opium substitutes with the intent to profit. Zhu Xirong, a repeat offender, is sentenced to two months of imprisonment for using opium substitutes. Sun Yuqing, Gu Yuanli, Wang Dianhua, Guo Gaoren, and Wu Guozhao are each sentenced to one month of imprisonment for using opium. The number of days of detention before the judgement is confirmed shall be deducted from the imprisonment at a rate of two days of detention for one day of imprisonment. Wang Dianhua, Guo Gaoren, and Wu Guozhao are each granted a two-year suspended sentence. Lu Guiguan is found not guilty. The opium paraphernalia is confiscated and destroyed.

▲Police Department versus Han Guisheng, et al., an opium case (Judgement): Han Guisheng is sentenced to six months of imprisonment for providing premises for others to use opium substitutes in his inn. Ye Mingshan, a repeat offender, is sentenced to two months of imprisonment for using opium substitutes. Yao Guixian is sentenced to one month of imprisonment for using opium substitutes. The number of days of detention before the judgement is confirmed shall be deducted from the imprisonment at a rate of two days of detention for one day of imprisonment. Yao Guixian is granted a two-year suspended sentence. The opium paraphernalia, etc., are confiscated and destroyed.

▲Police Department versus Cai A'er, et al., a theft and stolen goods case (Judgement): Cai A'er is sentenced to two months of imprisonment for repeated theft. The number of days of detention before the judgement is confirmed shall be deducted from the imprisonment at a rate of two days of detention for one day of imprisonment. Lin Jinfeng is fined 100 yuan for dealing with stolen goods. If unable to pay, he shall be imprisoned for one day for every two yuan. The number of days of detention before the judgement is confirmed shall be deducted from the fine at a rate of one day of detention for two yuan of the fine. Deng Baohe is found not guilty.

▲Police Department versus Lu A'tu, a gambling case (Judgement): Lu A'tu is sentenced to one month of imprisonment for assisting in gathering people to gamble with the intent to profit, and is fined 120 yuan. If unable to pay, he shall be imprisoned for one day for every two yuan. The number of days of detention before the judgement is confirmed shall be deducted from the imprisonment at a rate of two days of detention for one day of imprisonment. The gambling money and lottery tickets are confiscated.

▲Criminal Judgments: In the case of Jin Dushi obstructing family (Main text) Jin Dushi is sentenced to six months imprisonment for enticing a woman under the age of twenty to leave her parental rights. The number of days in detention shall be used as a two-day reduction for one day of imprisonment.▲In the case of Zhu Wenxiang obstructing family, (Main text) Zhu Wenxiang is sentenced to six months imprisonment for enticing a woman under the age of twenty with the intention of adultery. The number of days in detention shall be used as a two-day reduction for one day of imprisonment.▲In the case of Wang Zhenyue robbery, (Main text) Wang Zhenyue is found not guilty.▲In the case of Shi Deqian and others disturbing order (Main text) Shi Deqian, Cao Xiaomao, Zhong Caisheng, and Ji Duguizhou are each sentenced to fifteen days of detention for using violence and coercion to force others to perform duties they were not obligated to perform. The number of days in detention shall be used as a two-day reduction for one day of detention.▲In the case of Yang Daode opium, (Main text) Yang Daode is sentenced to six months imprisonment and fined one hundred and fifty yuan for possessing opium with the intention to sell. If the fine is not fully paid after compulsory execution, one yuan will be converted to one day of imprisonment in lieu of the fine. The number of days in detention shall be used as a two-day reduction for one day of imprisonment.▲Ruling of this court prosecutor regarding the unnamed opium case (Main text) The 21 taels of opium, 53 boxes of red pills, 72 bags of cigarette pills, and 1 bag of cigarette powder are confiscated.▲In the case of Chen Chenshi murder, (Main text) Chen Chenshi is sentenced to ten years imprisonment and deprived of civil rights for twelve years for murder. The number of days in detention shall be used as a two-day reduction for one day of imprisonment. Chen Chenshi shall compensate Pang Hanqing for funeral expenses of 384 yuan in foreign currency.▲In the case of Hua Shunkui embezzlement (Main text) Fei Jinling is found not guilty. The related civil suit is dismissed.▲In the case of Zhou Heyuan stolen goods, (Main text) Zhou Heyuan, Xu Shanchang, Dui Chaoji, Yao Xingzhuo, and Wu Wanyuan are each sentenced to three months imprisonment for jointly selling stolen goods. The number of days in detention shall be used as a two-day reduction for one day of imprisonment.▲In the case of Xiang Dao Zui and others bribery, (Main text) Xiang Dao and Jing Huashangui are granted immunity. The case of Li Liancai suing Cai Zhushi and others for injury, (Main text) This private prosecution is not accepted. The case of Shen Hushi suing Zhu Liankui and others for injury, (Main text) This private prosecution is not accepted.▲Ruling on the case of Ji Kaiyuan suing Wang Zai Shi and others for false accusation and defamation (Main text) This private prosecution is dismissed.▲In the case of Yu Jiyan suing Liu Yifan and others for fraud (Main text) Liu Yifan and Wu Yizhai are both found not guilty.▲In the case of Qu Ajin and others destroying newspapers (Main text) This public prosecution is not accepted.▲In the case of Li Xiaosanzi theft (Main text) Li Xiaosanzi is sentenced to six months imprisonment for burglary at night. The number of days in detention shall be used as a two-day reduction for one day of imprisonment.▲In the case of Li Bingxiang theft (Main text) Li Bingxiang is sentenced to six months imprisonment for burglary at night. The number of days in detention shall be used as a two-day reduction for one day of imprisonment.▲In the case of Cheng Zhangmu injury (Main text) This public prosecution is not accepted.▲Ruling of this court prosecutor regarding the Qian Guoxiu opium appeal case (Main text) The trial of this case is suspended.▲In the case of Sun Dongsong theft (Main text) Sun Dongsong is found not guilty.▲In the case of Wang Ranji suing Gao Sihai and others for unlawful detention and injury (Main text) This private prosecution is not accepted.▲In the case of Fu Jitao suing Fu Fuxin for fraud (Main text) This private prosecution is not accepted.▲In the case of Li Jixian embezzlement (Main text) Li Jixian is fined fifty yuan for embezzling property he possessed but belonged to others. If the fine is not fully paid after compulsory execution, one yuan will be converted to one day of imprisonment in lieu of the fine. The number of days in detention shall be used as a one-day reduction for one yuan of the fine.▲In the case of Lin Huichun counterfeit currency (Main text) Lin Huichun is fined thirty yuan for receiving and knowingly using counterfeit currency. If the fine is not fully paid after compulsory execution, one yuan will be converted to one day of imprisonment in lieu of the fine. The number of days in detention shall be used as a one-day reduction for one yuan of the fine. The three yuan of counterfeit currency is confiscated.▲In the case of Chen Maowen theft (Main text) Chen Maowen is fined seventy yuan for theft. If the fine is not fully paid after compulsory execution, one yuan will be converted to one day of imprisonment in lieu of the fine. The number of days in detention shall be used as a one-day reduction for one yuan of the fine.▲In the case of Zhou Hongyuan and others stolen goods (Main text) Zhou Heyuan, Xu Xiaochang, Ma Chaoji, Yao Xingzhuo, and Wu Wanyuan are each sentenced to three months imprisonment for jointly knowingly buying stolen goods. The number of days in detention shall be used as a two-day reduction for one day of imprisonment.▲In the case of Chen Guobin opium (Main text) Chen Guobin is sentenced to two months imprisonment and fined twenty yuan for smoking opium. If the fine is not fully paid after compulsory execution, one yuan will be converted to one day of imprisonment in lieu of the fine. The number of days in detention shall be used as a two-day reduction for one day of imprisonment. The opium paraphernalia is confiscated.▲In the case of Yang Chuanbao and others obstructing family (Main text) Yang Chuanbao and Xue Xiaoshan are each sentenced to six months imprisonment for jointly enticing a woman under the age of twenty. The number of days in detention shall be used as a two-day reduction for one day of imprisonment.▲Civil Judgments:▲In the case of Bao Maomao vs. Chen Fuquan document delivery appeal (Main text) The original judgment is overturned. The appellee's claim in the first instance is dismissed. Litigation costs for both the first and second instances are to be borne by the appellee.▲In the case of 苪鹤鸣 (Bing Heming) and others vs. 金月华 (Jin Yuehua) debt case (Main text) The defendant 金月华 (Jin Yuehua) shall repay the plaintiff 黃鹤鸣 (Huang Heming) silver 2147 taels, 9 qian, 4 fen, and foreign currency 180 yuan, plus annual interest of 6% from July 1, 1932, until the date of execution. She shall also repay the plaintiff 杨兴祥 (Yang Xingxiang) silver 2000 taels, plus interest at the agreed rate of 1.2% per month from November 19, 1931, until the date of execution. The remainder of the plaintiff Huang Heming's claim is dismissed. Litigation costs are to be borne by the defendant.▲In the case of 顾佘氏 (Gu Sheshi) vs. 顾业臣 (Gu Yechen) consolation money and living expenses case (Main text) The plaintiff's claim is dismissed. Litigation costs are to be borne by the plaintiff.▲In the case of Zhou Shengquan vs. Zhou Ronglin and others confirmation of ownership (Main text) The land located at No. 99, Rongzi Wei, 19th division, 1st district, 23rd bao, measuring 2 fen and 4 li, is confirmed to be owned by the plaintiff. Litigation costs are to be borne jointly by the defendants.▲In the case of Zhou Songzhi vs. Zhou Hehe and others execution objection (Main text) The plaintiff's claim is dismissed. Litigation costs are to be borne by the plaintiff.▲In the case of 恊豐順煤號號 (Xie Fengshun Coal Company) vs. 余天韵 (Yu Tianyun) for goods payment (Main text) The defendant shall repay the plaintiff goods payment of 181 yuan in foreign currency. Litigation costs are to be borne by the defendant.▲In the case of Liu Wenxuan and others vs. Lu Weizhang shore fees appeal (Main text) The appeal is dismissed. Second instance litigation costs are to be borne by the appellant.▲In the case of Chen Quansheng vs. Chen Jindao property division case (Main text) The plaintiff's claim is dismissed. Litigation costs are to be borne by the plaintiff.▲Ruling on the case of Cai Heyun vs. Tan Shunjuan for debt retrial (Main text) The retrial is dismissed. Retrial litigation costs are to be borne by the retrial plaintiff.▲In the case of He Shaoji vs. Feng Qiuxin land price (Main text) The defendant shall return 700 yuan to the plaintiff. Litigation costs are to be borne by the defendant for three-quarters and the plaintiff for one-quarter.▲In the case of Zhou Keji and Lu Zhankui returning foreign currency (Main text) The plaintiff's claim is dismissed. Litigation costs are to be borne by the plaintiff.▲In the case of Wang Rongchu vs. Gu Zhaoqi and others rent case (Main text) The defendants Gu Zhaoqi, Yue Yuanxing, and Li Zhangshi shall each pay the plaintiff rent of 27 yuan and 5 jiao in foreign currency, plus 35 jiao in small foreign currency. Du Guangcai shall pay the plaintiff rent of 32 yuan in foreign currency, plus 42 jiao in small foreign currency. Wang Zhengyi shall pay the plaintiff rent of 22 yuan in foreign currency, plus 28 jiao in small foreign currency. All shall vacate the premises. Litigation costs are to be borne equally by the defendants.▲In the case of Ding Bohua vs. Qiu Shi and others rent case (Main text) The defendant Qiu Shi shall pay the plaintiff rent of 162 yuan in foreign currency and shall vacate the premises. If she is unable to pay the rent, it shall be paid by the defendant Kong Changyu Company. Litigation costs, except for one-third of the withdrawn portion borne by the plaintiff, are to be borne by the defendant Qiu Shi for two-thirds.▲In the case of Wang Pinxiang vs. Liu Fugen base land case (Main text) The plaintiff's claim is dismissed. Litigation costs are to be borne by the plaintiff.▲Ruling on the case of Yang Hongji vs. Chen Yusheng and others loan case (Main text) The plaintiff's claim is dismissed. Jiangsu High Court Second Branch 215

Criminal Judgments: In the case of Chen Decai and others regarding gambling (Main text) The appeal is rejected.▲In the case of Ma Zide regarding endangering the Republic of China (Main text) Ma Zide is sentenced to two years and six months imprisonment for organizing a group with the aim of endangering the Republic of China. The number of days in detention before the judgment is finalized shall be used as a two-day reduction for one day of imprisonment. Documents with reactionary meaning are confiscated.▲In the case of Xiang Jinmao regarding the defendant's robbery (Main text) The original judgment is revoked. Mao Xiangjin is sentenced to four years imprisonment for robbery. The number of days in detention before the judgment is finalized shall be used as a two-day reduction for one day of imprisonment. Civil Judgments: In the case of Yin Sunshi vs. China Aviation Company regarding compensation (Main text) The original judgment is changed. The appellee shall compensate the appellants 15,000 yuan in foreign currency. The remainder of the appeal is rejected. The appellee shall bear 3/10 of the litigation costs for the first and second instances. The appellants shall bear the remainder. In the case of Hu Rongzhang vs. Cao Yangshi regarding debt repayment appeal (Main text) The appeal is rejected. The appellant shall bear the litigation costs for the second instance. (Above, August 11th)

Civil Ruling: Regarding the case of Yan Ziliang and others vs. Qin Cainan for requesting payment of debt (Main text) The appeal is rejected. The appellant shall bear the litigation costs for the second instance. (Above, August 11th)
